# Welcome | OF-Scraper

OF-Scraper is a command-line tool that lets you download media from OnlyFans and perform bulk actions like liking or unliking posts

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper#installation)

# Installing Prerequisites | OF-Scraper

This page outlines how to install the necessary tools and Python versions required to run OF-Scraper outside of Docker.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/pre-install-guide#getting-uv)

Getting UV


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

UV is a modern, fast Python package installer and dependency resolver. It's the recommended tool for managing OF-Scraper installations.

circle-info

Installing UV with one of their official installation scripts is recommended for the most straightforward setup.

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdocs.astral.sh%2Fstatic%2Fapple-touch-icon.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=481e89b9&sv=2)Installation | uvdocs.astral.shchevron-right](https://docs.astral.sh/uv/getting-started/installation/)

[PreviousInstallchevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation)
[NextUV Installchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/uv-install)

# UV Install | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/uv-install#installing-uv)

Installing UV


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

Important: UV is a standalone binary. You do not need Python installed on your system to install UV. Once UV is installed, it can then manage and install Python versions for you. Installing UV with one of their official installation scripts is recommended for the most straightforward setup.

[Installing Prerequisites](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/pre-install-guide)

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/uv-install#installing-upgrading-of-scraper)

Installing/Upgrading OF-Scraper


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**Tip: Use the** `**--verbose**` **command to get more details about the install process.**

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/uv-install#stable-release-install)

**Stable Release Install**

To install the latest stable release of OF-Scraper:

Copy

    uv tool install ofscraper --force

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/uv-install#development-release)

Development Release

**Pre-release**

To install the latest pre-release version:

Copy

    uv tool install --prerelease allow ofscraper --force

**Development**

To install the very latest development version directly from the GitHub repository:

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/uv-install#specific-version-of-script)

Specific Version of Script

To install a specific stable or pre-release version of the script:

Replace `<version>` with the exact version number you want to install (e.g., `ofscraper==2.4.3`).

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/uv-install#specific-version-of-python)

Specific Version of Python

You can specify the Python version `uv` should use for the tool installation by appending `--python <version_number>` to your command.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/uv-install#including-pyffmpeg-optional)

Including pyffmpeg (Optional)

pyffmpeg is a Python package that provides ffmpeg capabilities directly within Python by bundling its own ffmpeg binaries. You can accomplish this by appending \[ffmpeg\] to the install name when using uv tool install.

example: `uv tool install ofscraper[ffmpeg] --force`

circle-info

When you install ofscraper using ofscraper\[ffmpeg\], pyffmpeg will be automatically installed as a dependency. pyffmpeg then manages its own ffmpeg binary for the script, meaning you generally do not need to separately install ffmpeg or mp4decrypt on your host system or mount them into Docker containers.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/uv-install#upgrade)

Upgrade

It's recommended to explicitly uninstall `ofscraper` before upgrading to avoid potential conflicts, as not doing so has caused problems for users previously.

To upgrade `ofscraper` to the latest stable release:

To upgrade `ofscraper` to the latest prerelease or development version:

[NextBinary Releaseschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/binary-releases)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    uv tool install git+https://github.com/datawhores/OF-Scraper.git --force

Copy

    uv tool install --prerelease allow ofscraper==<version>

Copy

    # Example: Install a specific script version with Python 3.12
    uv tool install --prerelease allow ofscraper==<version> --python 3.12

Copy

    uv tool uninstall ofscraper # Recommended first step
    uv tool install ofscraper --force

Copy

    uv tool uninstall ofscraper # Recommended first step
    uv tool install --prerelease allow ofscraper --force

# Install from source | OF-Scraper

This guide provides instructions for installing and setting up the project from source.

**Important Note for Developers:** This project uses a custom versioning scheme for development builds that may not strictly adhere to PEP 440 for PyPI. This guide includes steps to manage that for local development.

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/install-from-source#prerequisites)

Prerequisites


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you begin, ensure you have the following installed on your system:

*   **Git:** For cloning the project repository.
    
    *   [Installation Guidearrow-up-right](https://git-scm.com/book/en/v2/Getting-Started-Installing-Git)
        
    
*   **uv:** A fast Python package installer and resolver.
    
    *   Follow the official installation instructions: [uv Installation Guidearrow-up-right](https://docs.astral.sh/uv/getting-started/installation/)
        
    

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/install-from-source#installation-steps)

Installation Steps


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Follow these steps to get your project up and running:

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/install-from-source#id-1.-clone-the-repository)

1\. Clone the Repository

First, clone the project from its Git repository:

Copy

    git clone https://github.com/datawhores/OF-Scraper/
    cd OF-Scraper

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/install-from-source#id-2.-pull-the-latest-tags)

2\. Pull the Latest Tags

To ensure you have access to all version information, pull the Git tags:

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/install-from-source#id-3.-prepare-environment-variables-for-custom-versioning)

3\. Prepare Environment Variables (for Custom Versioning)

The project uses a custom versioning strategy for local development and CI/CD that overrides the default PEP 440 checks during the build process. You need to source a script to set the necessary environment variables:

Bash

This script will set variables that allow Hatch to correctly interpret and build the project's development versions.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/install-from-source#id-4.-create-a-python-virtual-environment)

4\. Create a Python Virtual Environment

It's highly recommended to use a virtual environment to isolate your project's dependencies from your system's Python installation. `uv` can create these for you:

Bash

This will create a new virtual environment named `.venv` (by default) in your project directory.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/install-from-source#id-5.-activate-the-virtual-environment)

5\. Activate the Virtual Environment

Before installing dependencies, you need to activate the virtual environment:

Bash

_(On Windows, you would typically use_ `_.\.venv\Scripts\activate_`_)_

You should see `(.venv) or OF-Scraper` or similar prefix in your terminal prompt, indicating the virtual environment is active.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/install-from-source#id-6.-install-project-dependencies)

6\. Install Project Dependencies

Now, use `uv` to install all project dependencies and reinstall any existing ones to ensure a clean state:

Bash

This command will read your `pyproject.toml` (or `requirements.txt`) and install all necessary packages into your activated virtual environment. The `--reinstall` flag ensures that if any packages are already present, they are reinstalled, which can be useful after pulling updates.

[PreviousRelease Infochevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/release-info)
[NextGetting Started and Settingschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started)

Last updated 9 months ago

    source scripts/commit_version.sh

    uv venv

    source .venv/bin/activate

    uv sync --reinstall

# Release Info | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/release-info#release-types)

Release Types


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

OF-Scraper uses distinct release types to indicate stability and origin.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/release-info#continuous-development-builds-snapshot-releases)

Continuous Development Builds (Snapshot Releases)

These releases are generated directly from recent commits on development branches (like `main`). They represent the absolute latest state of the codebase and typically include a commit hash in their name.

*   Naming Convention: Often includes a branch name, a short commit hash, and the **date of the associated commit for chronological sorting** (e.g., 3.13.dev8-a70aca3e)
    
*   **Stability:** These are bleeding-edge versions and may contain new features, bug fixes, or unresolved issues. They are primarily for testing and development.
    
*   **Example Tag:** `main-9e54ed3-1749940070`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/release-info#pre-release-versions-e.g.-x.y.z.devn)

Pre-release Versions (e.g., `X.Y.Z.devN`)

These releases are designated as "semi-stable" and are pushed for broader testing before a full stable release. They typically follow a `major.minor.patch.devN` numbering scheme.

*   **Naming Convention:** Follows the format `major.minor.patch.devN` (e.g., `3.7.0.dev0`).
    
*   **Stability:** More stable than continuous development builds, but still undergoing testing.
    
*   **Example Version:** `3.7.0.dev0`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/release-info#stable-releases-numbered)

Stable Releases (Numbered)

These are production-ready versions of OF-Scraper, thoroughly tested and considered stable for general use. They mark a specific commit as a reliable release point.

*   **Naming Convention:** Standard semantic versioning (e.g., `X.Y.Z`, like `3.6.0`).
    
*   **Stability:** Highly stable and recommended for most users.
    
*   **Example Version:** `3.6.0`
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/release-info#release-distributions)

Release Distributions


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/release-info#python-package)

Python Package

Stable and pre-release versions of the Python package are hosted on **PyPI**

For a comprehensive history of all releases (including pre-releases), visit the official PyPI page:

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fpypi.org%2Fstatic%2Fimages%2Ffavicon.35549fe8.ico&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6520cf72&sv=2)ofscraperPyPIchevron-right](https://pypi.org/project/ofscraper/#history)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/release-info#docker-images)

Docker Images

Stable, pre-release, and dev versions of multi-arch Docker images are hosted on **GitHub Container Registry** and **Docker Hub**

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhub.docker.com%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b678431&sv=2)datawhores/of-scraper - Docker Imagehub.docker.comchevron-right](https://hub.docker.com/r/datawhores/of-scraper/tags)

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Ffluidicon.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc891f14&sv=2)GitHubGitHubchevron-right](https://github.com/datawhores/OF-Scraper/pkgs/container/of-scraper)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/release-info#binaries)

Binaries

Stable, pre-release, and dev versions are released as binaries on **GitHub** for Windows, macOS, and Linux

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Ffluidicon.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc891f14&sv=2)Releases · datawhores/OF-ScraperGitHubchevron-right](https://github.com/datawhores/OF-Scraper/releases)

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/release-info#release-files)

Release Files

Binaries include various file types **compatible with different platforms**

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/release-info#example-files)

Example Files

Below is an illustrative list of files you might find in a release, with common naming patterns.

*   `ofscraper_windows_x64.zip` (Windows zips)
    
*   `ofscraper_linux` (Linux script)

Before Starting


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The guide assumes you have your terminal program open and have already installed Python. If you're unsure about this, follow this guide

[Installing Prerequisiteschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/pre-install-guide)

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation#install-via-a-package-manager)

Install via a package manager


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**pipx is recommended for its virtual environment management capabilities.**

**It serves as an abstraction layer over pip, placing installed scripts within isolated virtual environments. This approach is highly recommended for script installation as it offers several advantages:**

*   **Prevents conflicts:** By isolating scripts and their dependencies within virtual environments, pipx effectively eliminates conflicts with other Python packages or system-wide installations.
    
*   **Enhances organization:** Each script resides in its own distinct virtual environment, promoting better organization and clarity in project management.
    
*   **Simplifies updates:** pipx streamlines the process of updating scripts, ensuring you always have access to the latest versions and features
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation#option-1-pipx-install)

**Option 1: PIPX Install**

[UV Installchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/uv-install)

Compiled Binaries \[No Install\]

circle-info

**A pyinstaller based binary is an executable file that contains your Python script and all the necessary dependencies to run it on different operating systems. Pyinstaller analyzes the script and bundles it with the Python interpreter, libraries, modules, and other resources into a single file or folder**

**Support for issues specific to how pyinstaller operates may be limited**

Windows

Copy

    C:/Users/username/.config/ofscraper/config.json

# Responsetype Placeholders | OF-Scraper

This feature enables you to group downloads using the 'responsetype' placeholder.

It allows combining various response types into a single folder or segregating downloads into separate folders based on their 'responsetype.'

For example, you can merge 'stories' and 'highlights' into one folder or categorize 'purchased' items and 'messages' into a folder named 'Premium.'

Another option is to organize 'timeline posts' into a separate folder labeled 'posts.'

The initial value indicates the mapped response type, which should remain unchanged. The second value determines the remapped 'responsetype.'

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options/remapping-responsetype#example)

Example

Copy

    "timeline": "posts",
    "message": "premium",
    "archived": "archived",
    "paid": "premium",
    "stories": "stories",
    "highlights": "stories",
     "profile": "profile"

Copy

    dir_format": "{model_username}/{responsetype}/{mediatype}/"

Copy

    timeline -> maps to posts -> files save to "{model_username}/Posts/{mediatype}/"
    messages -> maps to premium -> files save to "{model_username}/Premium/{mediatype}/"
    archived -> maps to archived -> files save to "{model_username}/Archived/{mediatype}/"
    paid -> maps to premium -> files save to "{model_username}/Premium/{mediatype}/"
    stories -> maps to stories -> files save to "{model_username}/Stories/{mediatype}/"
    highlight -> maps to stories  -> files save to "{model_username}/Stories/{mediatype}/"
    profile -> maps to archived  -> files save to "{model_username}/Profile/{mediatype}/"

These default settings are crafted to ensure maximum compatibility with Digitalcriminal's script.

[PreviousPlaceholderschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options/customizing-save-path)
[NextDownload Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Example Configs | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/example-configs#example-1)

Example 1


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    {
        "config": {
            "main_profile": "main_profile",
            "metadata": "{configpath}/{profile}/.data/{model_username}_{model_id}",
            "discord": "",
            "file_options": {
                "save_location": "/home/james/Data/ofscraper",
                "dir_format": "/{model_username}/{responsetype}/{mediatype}/",
                "file_format": "{filename}.{ext}",
                "textlength": 0,
                "space-replacer": " ",
                "date": "MM-DD-YYYY",
                "text_type_default": "letter",
                "truncation_default": true
            },
            "download_options": {
                "file_size_limit": 0,
                "file_size_min": 0,
                "filter": [\
                    "Images",\
                    "Audios",\
                    "Videos"\
                ],
                "auto_resume": false,
                "system_free_min": 0,
                "number_retries": 10
            },
            "binary_options": {
                "mp4decrypt": "/home/james/.config/ofscraper/bin/mp4decrypt",
                "ffmpeg": "/home/james/.config/ofscraper/bin/ffmpeg"
            },
            "cdm_options": {
                "private-key": "/home/james/.config/ofscraper/device/private_key.pem",
                "client-id": "/home/james/.config/ofscraper/device/client_id.bin",
                "key-mode-default": "manual",
            },
            "performance_options": {
                "download-sems": 10,
                "threads": 10
            },
            "advanced_options": {
                "code-execution": true,
                "dynamic-mode-default": "dc",
                "backend": "aio",
                "downloadbars": false,
                "cache-mode": "sqlite",
                "appendlog": false,
                "custom_values":null
                "sanitize_text": false,
                "avatar": true,
                "temp_dir": null
            },
            "responsetype": {
                "timeline": "Posts",
                "message": "Messages",
                "archived": "Archived",
                "paid": "Messages",
                "stories": "Stories",
                "highlights": "Stories",
                "profile": "Profile",
                "pinned": "Posts"
            }
        }
    }

# Docker | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#volumes)

Volumes


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

**If manually downloading binaries, you'll need to mount the Linux-based binaries from your host system into the container. Refer to the 'Docker Compose' section for examples.**

Mount Point

Purpose

Typical Default Location

**APP\_HOME**

The **home directory** for your application's user inside the container. This often serves as the base for other default paths.

`/home/<APP_USER>` (e.g., `/home/ofscraper`)

**DATA\_DIR**

Where the application stores its **persistent data files**, such as databases, downloaded content, or user-generated media.

`$APP_HOME/data` (e.g., `/home/ofscraper/data`)

**CONFIG\_DIR**

Where the application stores its **configuration files** and settings.

`$APP_HOME/.config` (e.g., `/home/ofscraper/.config`)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#config_dir)

CONFIG\_DIR

The `CONFIG_DIR` is where OF-Scrapers configuration files will be stored. It will prioritizes any explicit setting by the user

Scenario

`CONFIG_DIR` Environment Variable

`APP_HOME` Value (Example)

`CONFIG_DIR` Final Path

Explanation

**1\. Explicitly Set**

`CONFIG_DIR=/app/onfig/`

`/home/ofscraper`

`/app/config`

If you explicitly provide the `CONFIG_DIR` environment variable, its value is used directly. This overrides any default behavior.

**2\. Not Set / Empty**

`CONFIG_DIR` is unset or `CONFIG_DIR=""`

`/home/ofscraper`

`/home/ofscraper/.config`

If `CONFIG_DIR` is not provided (or provided as an empty string), it defaults to a hidden `.config` directory within the determined `APP_HOME`.

or users `Home`

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#data_dir)

DATA\_DIR

The `DATA_DIR` is where your application will store its persistent data. Similar to `CONFIG_DIR`, it will respects user overrides.

Scenario

`DATA_DIR` Environment Variable

`APP_HOME` Value (Example)

`DATA_DIR` Final Path

Explanation

**1\. Explicitly Set**

`DATA_DIR=/app/data`

`/home/ofscraper`

`/app/data`

If you explicitly provide the `DATA_DIR` environment variable, its value is used directly, overriding any default.

**2\. Not Set / Empty**

`DATA_DIR` is unset or `DATA_DIR=""`

`/home/ofscraper`

`/home/ofscraper/data`

If `DATA_DIR` is not provided (or provided as an empty string), it defaults to a `data` directory within the determined `APP_HOM`

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#home-folder)

Home Folder

triangle-exclamation

**If you do** _**not**_ **explicitly set the** `**HOME_FOLDER**` **environment variable, the script's default behavior is to make the home directory name match the adapted** `**APP_USER**` **name. For instance, if** `**APP_USER**` **was initially** `**ofscraper**` **but gets adapted to an existing user like** `**nginx**` **(due to a UID conflict), the** `**APP_HOME**` **folder will dynamically change to** `**/home/nginx**`**. This keeps the user's name and home folder consistent within the container's** `**/etc/passwd**` **file.**

Scenario

`HOME_FOLDER` Environment Variable Status

`APP_USER` Adaptation (e.g., from `ofscraper` to `nginx`)

Resulting `APP_HOME` Directory Path in Container (`/etc/passwd`)

Explanation

**Default**

**Not set** (or empty string)

**Yes**, `APP_USER` changes

`/home/nginx` (dynamically matches new `APP_USER`)

When `HOME_FOLDER` isn't specified, the home directory name **automatically updates** to match the new `APP_USER` name if the user account has to adapt to an existing UID on the host. This keeps the user name and home folder consistent.

**Not set** (or empty string)

**No**, `APP_USER` remains `ofscraper`

`/home/ofscraper`

If no `HOME_FOLDER` is set and `APP_USER` doesn't need to change, the home directory defaults to `/home/ofscraper`.

**Explicit**

**Set** (e.g., `mydata`)

**Yes**, `APP_USER` changes

`/home/mydata` (remains as explicitly set)

If you explicitly define `HOME_FOLDER`, the home directory path **stays fixed** at `/home/mydata`. It will not change, even if `APP_USER` adapts to a different name due to UID/GID conflicts. This provides a stable, predictable home path.

**Set** (e.g., `mydata`)

**No**, `APP_USER` remains `ofscraper`

`/home/mydata`

The explicitly set `HOME_FOLDER` always takes precedence, so the home directory will be `/home/mydata`.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#environment-variables)

Environment Variables


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The container is managed by a entrypoint script that automatically creates a non-root user to run the application.

You can control the user, group, paths, and script behavior using the environment variables below.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#user-and-group-identity)

User and Group Identity

These variables control the identity of the user that runs the application inside the container.

For the best experience with mounted volumes, it is **highly recommended** to set `UID` and `GID` to match your host system's user (e.g., `-e UID=$(id -u) -e GID=$(id -g)`).

**Environment Variable**

**Default Value (if not set)**

**Purpose & Effect of Changing the Value**

`UID`

`1000`

Sets the **numeric User ID (UID)** for the application user, which is critical for matching file ownership on mounted volumes. Setting `UID=$(id -u)` makes the container user have the _same UID as your host user_, ensuring files it creates are correctly owned by you on the host. if the UID already exists with a different username in the container, it will adapt and use that existing user.

`GID`

`1000`

Sets the **numeric Group ID (GID)** for the application user's primary group, which works with `UID` to manage correct group ownership. Setting `GID=$(id -g)` ensures file permissions align with your host's primary group. Similar to `UID`, the script will adapt if this GID already belongs to an existing group.

`USERNAME`

`ofscraper`

Defines the **name** of the user to be created or managed inside the container. If you set `USERNAME=youruser`, the script will attempt to create or modify a user named `youruser` with the specified `UID`. This name is mainly for logical identification. If the `UID` you provide is already taken by a different user, the script will use that existing user's name instead and print a log message.

`GROUPNAME`

The value of `USERNAME`

Defines the **name** of the primary group for the application user. By default, the group name will match the username (e.g., `ofscraper`). You can set this explicitly if you have specific group naming conventions. Like `USERNAME`, this is secondary to `GID`.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#path-and-directory-management)

Path and Directory Management

These variables allow you to control where the application stores its files. This is useful for mounting specific host directories.

**Environment Variable**

**Default Value (if not set)**

**Purpose & Effect of Changing the Value**

`HOME_FOLDER`

The value of `USERNAME`

Sets the **folder name** for the user's home directory inside the container's `/home/` directory. If you set `USERNAME=john` and leave this unset, the home directory will be `/home/john`. If you set `HOME_FOLDER=my_app`, the home directory becomes `/home/my_app`, regardless of the `USERNAME`.

`DATA_DIR`

`$APP_HOME/data`

Overrides the path for the application's data directory. By default, data is stored in a `data` folder inside the user's home directory (e.g., `/home/ofscraper/data`). You can set this to any absolute path, such as `/data`, if you prefer to mount a volume directly to `/data`.

`CONFIG_DIR`

`$APP_HOME/.config`

Overrides the path for the application's configuration directory. By default, configuration is stored in a hidden `.config` folder inside the user's home directory (e.g., `/home/ofscraper/.config`). You can set this to an absolute path like `/config` to mount a volume there instead.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#script-behavior-flags)

Script Behavior Flags

These variables act as on/off switches to control specific actions within the entrypoint script.

**Environment Variable**

**Default Value (if not set)**

**Purpose & Effect of Changing the Value**

`KEEP_PERM`

`false`

Prevents the script from changing ownership of the home, data, and config directories. If you set `KEEP_PERM=true`, the script will **not** run `chown` on your mounted directories. This is useful for advanced setups like rootless Docker or when you are managing permissions manually on the host.

`SKIP_FFMPEG`

`false`

Controls the installation of the `pyffmpeg` Python package. If you set `SKIP_FFMPEG=true`, the script will not attempt to install the `pyffmpeg` package. This can be used to speed up container startup if you do not need its functionality or if the installation is causing issues.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#docker-run)

Docker Run


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This section provides the basic `docker run` commands to get OF-Scraper started. Remember to replace `/your/host/config/path/` with the actual path on your host machine where you want to store OF-Scraper's configuration, and `/your/host/data/path/` with where you want to store downloaded content. Replace `{args}` with your desired OF-Scraper commands (e.g., `ofscraper --username myonlyfans`)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#minimal-docker-run-command)

Minimal `docker run` Command

This command uses the container's default user and group settings (`ofscraper` user with UID/GID `1000`).

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#using-optional-environment-variables)

Using Optional Environment Variables

To pass these optional variables, add them to your `docker run` command using the `-e` flag:

Bash

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#docker-compose)

Docker Compose


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For more complex setups or for defining your service persistently, use Docker Compose. Remember to install `ffmpeg` and `mp4decrypt` on your local system if you choose to mount them from the host.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#interactive-use)

Interactive Use

If you've set up your `docker-compose.yml` for interactive use (by using `command: ["/bin/bash", "-c", "sleep infinity"]` or similar), you'll start the container in the background and then execute commands inside it.

To run the scraper manually (after bringing the service up with `docker compose up -d` to start it in detached mode), use:

Bash

Replace `{args}` with your desired OF-Scraper commands, for example: `docker compose exec -it ofscraper ofscraper --username myuser --posts all`.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#building-custom-images)

Building Custom Images


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**All officially released OF-Scraper Docker images already include** `**ffmpeg**` **built-in.**

This section is **only relevant if you are building the OF-Scraper Docker image locally from source**, for instance, to include specific Python dependencies or to customize the build process. You can use `docker buildx` for this.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/installation/docker#using-install_ffmpeg-build-argument)

Using `INSTALL_FFMPEG` Build Argument

The OF-Scraper `Dockerfile` includes an `ARG` (build argument) named `INSTALL_FFMPEG`. When set to `true` during a local build, this argument triggers the installation of the `pyffmpeg` Python package, which in turn includes and manages its own `ffmpeg` binary within the container.

To build an image locally where `pyffmpeg` (and thus `ffmpeg`) is included, you would pass `INSTALL_FFMPEG=true` to your `docker buildx` command:

circle-info

**Benefit of built-in FFmpeg:** If your image was built with `INSTALL_FFMPEG=true` (or if you're using an official released image that already includes FFmpeg), the image is self-contained. This means you generally **do not need to install** `**ffmpeg**` **on your host system or mount it into your Docker container**

Copy

    docker run -it --rm --name=ofscraper \
      -v /your/host/config/path/:/home/ofscraper/.config/ofscraper/ \
      -v /your/host/data/path/:/home/ofscraper/data \
      ghcr.io/datawhores/of-scraper:main ofscraper {args}

Copy

    docker run -it --rm --name=ofscraper \
      -v /your/host/config/path/:/home/ofscraper/.config/ofscraper/ \
      -v /your/host/data/path/:/home/ofscraper/data \
      -e USER_NAME=youruser \
      -e USER_ID=$(id -u) \
      -e GROUP_ID=$(id -g) \
      -e GROUP_NAME=yourgroup \ # Optional: Only if you want a custom group name different from USER_NAME
      ghcr.io/datawhores/of-scraper:main ofscraper {args}

Copy

    version: "3.8" # Recommended to use a recent version for new features
    services:
      of-scraper:
        stdin_open: true # Keeps STDIN open for interactive processes
        tty: true # Allocates a pseudo-TTY for a terminal-like interface
        container_name: ofscraper
        
        environment: # Optional environment variables
          # These are recommended for correct file permissions on mounted volumes.
          # Default UID/GID is 1000:1000 if not specified via environment variables in your shell.
          # - USER_NAME=ofscraper   # Defaults to 'ofscraper' in the entrypoint script
          # - USER_ID=${USER_ID}   # Host user's UID (e.g., set via 'export USER_ID=$(id -u)' on host)
          # - GROUP_ID=${GROUP_ID} # Host user's GID (e.g., set via 'export GROUP_ID=$(id -g)' on host)
          # - GROUP_NAME=mygroup # Optional: If you want a custom group name different from USER_NAME
        volumes:
          # Mount your configuration directory (replace ./config/ with your host path)
          - ./config/:/home/ofscraper/.config/ofscraper/
          # Mount your data storage directory (replace ./data/ with your host path)
          - ./data/:/home/ofscraper/data/
          # Optional: Mount pre-installed binaries from host (adjust paths as needed)
          # - /usr/bin/ffmpeg:/usr/bin/ffmpeg
    
        image: ghcr.io/datawhores/of-scraper:main 
        # --- COMMAND OPTIONS ---
        # Choose one of the following 'command' configurations based on your use case.
        # Uncomment the desired option and ensure others are commented out.
    
        # Option 1: For interactive use (recommended if you frequently run commands manually)
        # This keeps the container running indefinitely in the background.
        command: ["/bin/bash", "-c", "sleep infinity"]
        # To bring the container up: `docker compose up -d`
        # Then, to run commands inside it: `docker compose exec -it ofscraper ofscraper {args}`
        # Example: `docker compose exec -it ofscraper ofscraper --username myuser`
    
        # Option 2: To run the scraper automatically with specific arguments when the container starts
        # Uncomment the line below and comment out Option 1 above.
        # command: "ofscraper --username ALL --posts all"
    
        # Optional: Configure restart policy.
        # restart: "unless-stopped" # Ensures the container restarts automatically unless explicitly stopped.

Copy

    docker compose exec -it ofscraper ofscraper {args}

    # Optional: Create a builder instance for multi-platform builds (recommended for cross-platform compatibility)
    # docker buildx create --name mybuilder --use

    # cd /path/to/OF-Scraper/repository

    docker buildx build --platform linux/amd64,linux/arm64 \
      --build-arg INSTALL_FFMPEG=true \
      -t my-ofscraper-image:latest \

Profile Menu

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F373772994-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FOlkVHnCqS3EnmDo4hGKm%252Fuploads%252FnwW2Endo4sngQPdqZk3J%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D970503e5-4934-4bb4-8866-f57b74300a74&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f665b24&sv=2)

# Binaries Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/binaries-options#ffmpeg)

ffmpeg


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is necessary to combine audio and video parts of files utilized with mp4decrypt, resulting in the final output file

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/binaries-options#download-sources)

Download Sources

Releases

####

# Auth | OF-Scraper

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#undefined)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**The best way to solve authentication issues is to join the discord, as this will allow you to confirm if may be a wide spread issue**

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#example)

Example


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**values are randomized, but should be somewhat similar in style to the example**

An example of what an auth file should typically look like

Copy

    {
        "auth": {
            "user_agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36",
            "x-bc": "fncx03r1ygvh26ezq4pe830l49xtj1a146e1x2av",
            "auth_id": "400000",
            "sess": "5pb18tyng144dqyzevbgfddnrz",
            "auth_uid_": "400000"
        }
    }

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#auto-methods)

Auto methods


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You have various options for fetching authentication info. If possible, I'd suggest going for the cookie helper option—it demands the least effort once it's set up.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#m-rcus-cookie-helper)

M-rcus Cookie Helper

Please follow the instructions provided here to install it in your browser

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Ffluidicon.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc891f14&sv=2)GitHub - M-rcus/OnlyFans-Cookie-Helper: An extension made to make it easier to copy the correct \`auth.json\` values when using https://github.com/datawhores/OF-ScraperGitHubchevron-right](https://github.com/M-rcus/OnlyFans-Cookie-Helper)

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fuser-images.githubusercontent.com%2F67020411%2F230731183-26a43e62-4385-4fd9-aee8-f75a7c2d33cb.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fdbdd79d&sv=2)

image

With the helper, all you need to do is copy and paste the output from the program.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#browser-extraction)

Browser Extraction

This method is probably the second simplest. However, not all information can be automatically extracted.

You'll still need to manually locate and provide the x-bc header and the User-Agent as demonstrated below.

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fraw.githubusercontent.com%2Ftaux1c%2Fonlyfans-scraper%2Fmain%2Fmedia%2Frequest_headers.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95ff5763&sv=2)

For more details, check out the manual section below.

You won't need to worry about extracting any cookie information with this choice

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#manual-methods)

Manual methods


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**You can also manually edit auth information in script**

With this option, you'll need to manually input all the required information

It's not too terrible. I'll walk you through how to get this info in the next parts.

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#step-one-creating-the-auth.json-file)

Step One: Creating the 'auth.json' File

You first need to run the program in order for the `auth.json` file to be created. To run it, simply type `ofscraper` in your terminal and hit enter. Because you don't have an `auth.json` file, the program will create one for you and then ask you to enter some information. Now we need to get that information.

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#step-two-getting-your-auth-info)

Step Two: Getting Your Auth Info

_**If you've already used DIGITALCRIMINAL's OnlyFans script, you can simply copy and paste the auth information from there to here.**_

Go to your [notification areaarrow-up-right](https://onlyfans.com/my/notifications)
 on OnlyFans. Once you're there, open your browser's developer tools. If you don't know how to do that, consult the following chart:

Operating System

Keys

macOS

cmd + opt + I

Windows

ctrl+shift+I

Linux

ctrl+shift+I

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#id-1.-getting-a-valid-requests)

**1\. Getting a valid requests**

Once you have your browser's developer tools open, your screen should look like the following:

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fraw.githubusercontent.com%2Ftaux1c%2Fonlyfans-scraper%2Fmain%2Fmedia%2Fbrowser_tools_open.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f179e6a&sv=2)

Click on the `Network` tab at the top of the browser tools:

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fraw.githubusercontent.com%2Ftaux1c%2Fonlyfans-scraper%2Fmain%2Fmedia%2Fnetwork_tab.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d3d1ed&sv=2)

Then click on `XHR` sub-tab inside of the `Network` tab:

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fraw.githubusercontent.com%2Ftaux1c%2Fonlyfans-scraper%2Fmain%2Fmedia%2Fxhr_tab.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b84b8d5&sv=2)

Once you're inside of the `XHR` sub-tab, refresh the page while you have your browser's developer tools open. After the page reloads, you should see a section titled `init` appear:

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fraw.githubusercontent.com%2Ftaux1c%2Fonlyfans-scraper%2Fmain%2Fmedia%2Finit.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b741185b&sv=2)

When you click on `init`, you should see a large sidebar appear. Make sure you're in the `Headers` section:

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fraw.githubusercontent.com%2Ftaux1c%2Fonlyfans-scraper%2Fmain%2Fmedia%2Fheaders.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7a69fdd5&sv=2)

Skip to step 2 if you have found init successfully otherwise read the next section

* * *

circle-info

**If init does not appear use any entry with the domain onlyfans.com**

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#examples)

**Examples**

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F373772994-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FOlkVHnCqS3EnmDo4hGKm%252Fuploads%252FpHssUteJNS5PX5pQlXcg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0b75566-b88e-4efd-b3c7-1d21c7392051&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=323de7e1&sv=2)

onlyfans.com

You may need to right click the header field to enable the domain column

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F373772994-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FOlkVHnCqS3EnmDo4hGKm%252Fuploads%252F174ncW0jWrwYI9SeLEvR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ea78084-c444-451b-87e8-e3fdf69f420f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=24ecffad&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#id-2.-getting-data-from-requests)

2\. Getting data from requests

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fraw.githubusercontent.com%2Ftaux1c%2Fonlyfans-scraper%2Fmain%2Fmedia%2Finit.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b741185b&sv=2)

After that, scroll down until you see a subsection called `Request Headers`. You should then see three important fields inside of the `Request Headers` subsection: `Cookie`, `User-Agent`, and `x-bc`

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fraw.githubusercontent.com%2Ftaux1c%2Fonlyfans-scraper%2Fmain%2Fmedia%2Frequest_headers.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95ff5763&sv=2)

Inside of the `Cookie` field, you will see a couple of important bits:

*   `sess=`
    
*   `auth_id=`
    
*   `auth_uid_=`
    

_Your_ `auth_uid_` _will only appear_ _**if you have 2FA (two-factor authentication) enabled**__. Also, keep in mind that your_ `auth_uid_` _will have numbers after the final underscore and before the equal sign (that's your auth\_id)._

You need everything _**after**_ the equal sign and everything _**before**_ the semi-colon for all of those bits.

Once you've copied the value for your `sess` cookie, go back to the program, paste it in, and hit enter. Now go back to your browser, copy the `auth_id` value, and paste it into the program and hit enter. Then go back to your browser, copy the `auth_uid_` value, and paste it into the program and hit enter (**leave this blank if you don't use 2FA!!!**).

Once you do that, the program will ask for your user agent. You should be able to find your user agent in a field called `User-Agent` below the `Cookie` field. Copy it and paste it into the program and hit enter.

After it asks for your user agent, it will ask for your `x-bc` token. You should also be able to find this in the `Request Headers` section.

You're all set and you can now use `ofscraper`.

[PreviousAdvanced config optionschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options)
[NextControlling Output/Logschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/controlling-output)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#undefined)
    
*   [Example](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#example)
    
*   [Auto methods](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#auto-methods)
    
*   [M-rcus Cookie Helper](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#m-rcus-cookie-helper)
    
*   [Browser Extraction](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#browser-extraction)

*   [2\. Getting data from requests](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth#id-2.-getting-data-from-requests)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    {
        "auth": {
            "sess": "",
            "auth_id": "",
            "auth_uniq_": "",
            "user_agent": "",
            "x-bc": ""
        }
    }

circle-info

# Advanced Customization | OF-Scraper

Environment variables are a way for advanced users to have more control over certain aspects of the program

**Default Values:** All environment variables keys are listed in the `ofscraper/utils/of_env/values` folder. This folder contains separate folders/files for different types of value

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/advanced-customization#configuration-precedence)

Configuration Precedence

When determining the final value for any configuration setting, the program follows a specific order of precedence. Items higher on this list will **override** items lower on the list:

* * *

1.  Explicit `.env` File (`--env-file` option): Values loaded from the `.env` file(s) specified by the `--env-file` option. If this option is provided multiple times on the command line (e.g., `cli --env-file a.env --env-file b.env`), all specified files are loaded in the order they are declared in the command. Values from files loaded later will take precedence over those from files loaded earlier. These values also override any conflicting values from earlier source.
    
2.  Automatic `.env` File (via `load_dotenv`): Values loaded from a default `.env` file. This is typically initiated by a function call within the application's source code (e.g., `load_dotenv()`). The function searches for the file starting in the current working directory, then moves up through parent directories until it is found.
    
3.  System Environment Variables: Values already set in your operating system's environment (e.g., via `export VAR=VALUE` on Linux/macOS, or `set VAR=VALUE` on Windows Command Prompt). These are present before any `.env` files are loaded.
    
4.  Hardcoded Defaults: Default values defined directly within the program's source code. These are used only if a setting is not found via any of the above methods.
    

[PreviousMigrating from Digitalcriminal's scriptchevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/migrating-from-digitalcriminals-script)
[NextUsing the Scraperchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper)

Last updated 9 months ago

# Media Filtering Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options/media-filtering-options#filter)

filter


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Determines the type of content you wish to download.

Copy

    Options are Images,Audios,Videos case insensitive

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options/media-filtering-options#file_size_limit)

file\_size\_limit


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the maximum allowable file size for downloads

*   ignored if 0 or None
    
*   provided value should be in bytes or human readable string like '10MB'
    

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options/media-filtering-options#file_size_min)

file\_size\_min


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the minimum allowable file size for downloads

*   ignored if 0 or None
    
*   provided value should be in bytes or human readable string like '10MB'
    

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options/media-filtering-options#length_max)

length\_max


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Limits processed items to media as long or longer then the given length

in seconds

*   ignored if 0
    
*   only used to filter videos
    

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options/media-filtering-options#length_min)

length\_min


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Limits processed items to media as short or shorter then the given length

in seconds

*   ignored if 0
    
*   only used to filter videos
    

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options/media-filtering-options#block_ads)

block\_ads


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

remove posts with based on built in AD regex

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options/media-filtering-options#max_post_count)

max\_post\_count


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The maximum number of items to process

*   [block\_ads](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options/media-filtering-options#block_ads)
    
*   [max\_post\_count](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options/media-filtering-options#max_post_count)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    r"(#(?:ad|ads|AD|advertising|sponsored|promotion)|trial|discount|exclusive\s+offer|giveaway|limited\s+time|\Buser\s+promo|shoutout|endorsement)"

# Username selection or Fuzzy Search | OF-Scraper

circle-info

**Fuzzy search is built to mimic fzf**

OF-Scraper applies a fuzzy search technique to simplify managing selected models. This approximate search aims to find strong matches for the string you input.

However, the challenge lies in determining which models are being selected.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/username-selection-or-fuzzy-search#selecting-a-model)

Selecting a model


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For all models

Copy

    Ctrl+R

For a single model you can hit

Copy

    END  |  HOME | PAGEUP | PAGEDOWN 

For all Models

Copy

    Ctrl+A

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/username-selection-or-fuzzy-search#getting-model-detail)

Getting Model Detail


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

only a limited amount of data can be shown be shown at a time As the prompt menu does not work well when the data goes past a single

To view all details for a model

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/username-selection-or-fuzzy-search#sorting-filtering-list)

Sorting/Filtering List


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You'll be able to adjust the filters which controls the appearance of models on the list and how they're sorted

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/username-selection-or-fuzzy-search#searching-the-list)

Searching the list


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It's as simple as typing, for instance, 'example.'

The outcome is based on your account and the filters you've implemented.

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fuser-images.githubusercontent.com%2F67020411%2F230736225-1b24a4b3-d56f-4297-88bd-63e2d4815990.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=41273d86&sv=2)

image

Entering '1' here filters out all other non-matching options, displaying only '1'.

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fuser-images.githubusercontent.com%2F67020411%2F230736203-c7e433f9-30a9-4c35-8615-8046b3d7d001.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e434edcf&sv=2)

image

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/username-selection-or-fuzzy-search#how-does-searching-effect-my-currently-select-models)

How does searching effect my currently select models?

It doesn't it only effects which models appear in the list for example

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fuser-images.githubusercontent.com%2F67020411%2F230736111-3581cc77-bca0-491f-b86c-fdd3bd1d6551.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af0c7175&sv=2)

image

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fuser-images.githubusercontent.com%2F67020411%2F230736159-bdc9f4ec-87d7-48ac-9099-81743b52c785.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=660b0108&sv=2)

image

In the second image, although my previously chosen options aren't visible, they're still selected,

As shown by the number in parentheses, denoting the count of selected options (3).

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/username-selection-or-fuzzy-search#unselecting)

Unselecting


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To remove a model, either change the filter to an empty string or input a filter that displays the specific model you wish to remove.

You can use the previously mentioned keys to toggle between selecting and unselecting models.

Use one of the keys below during the model selection for up to date keys

# CDM issues | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options/cdm-issues#protobuff-issue)

protobuff issue


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    TypeError: Descriptors cannot not be created directly.
    If this call came from a _pb2.py file, your generated code is out of date and 
    must be regenerated with protoc >= 3.19.0.
    If you cannot immediately regenerate your protos, some other possible workarounds are:
    
     1. Downgrade the protobuf package to 3.20.x or lower.
     2. Set PROTOCOL_BUFFERS_PYTHON_IMPLEMENTATION=python (but this will use pure-Python parsing and will be much slower).
    

[https://forum.videohelp.com/threads/408031-Dumping-Your-own-L3-CDM-with-Android-Studio/page9#post2697726arrow-up-right](https://forum.videohelp.com/threads/408031-Dumping-Your-own-L3-CDM-with-Android-Studio/page9#post2697726)

[NextFAQ/Common Issueschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq)

# Placeholders | OF-Scraper

circle-exclamation

**If you want to recheck files --metadata-update after updating the config**

chevron-rightWindows path warning[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options/customizing-save-path#windows-path-warning)

`**\ should be escaped or replaced with a \\ or /**`

`**Not doing this could lead to an error**`

`**Examples:**`

Copy

    C:\Users\John.config\ofscraper\bin\ffmpeg.exe => 

Copy

    C:\Users\John.config\ofscraper\bin\ffmpeg.exe => 
    C:/Users/John.config/ofscraper/bin/ffmpeg.exe

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options/customizing-save-path#example-of-generated-filenames)

Example of generated filenames


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The placeholders described below will substitute the {} values

[Example Configschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/example-configs)

Copy

    "file_options": {
                "save_location": "/home/james/Data/ofscraper",
                "dir_format": "/{model_username}/{responsetype}/{mediatype}/",
                "file_format": "{filename}.{ext}",
                "textlength": 0,
                "space-replacer": " ",
                "date": "MM-DD-YYYY",
                "text_type_default": "letter",
                "truncation_default": true
            },

The generated filename based on the example config would be

* * *

circle-info

**Placeholders are generally the same between options here**

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options/customizing-save-path#dir_path-and-filename)

dir\_path and filename


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**You may use placeholders without any underscores (\_)**

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options/customizing-save-path#dir_path)

dir\_path

The relative directory path within the save location where files are stored

circle-info

**No unique placeholders**

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options/customizing-save-path#filename)

filename

The file's name segment in the saved file

circle-info

**When configuring filenames, ensure a unique element such as text, media ID, post ID, or filename is added to avoid naming conflict**

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options/customizing-save-path#text-placeholders)

Text Placeholders


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**Text mediatype will most likely need a overwrite to work properly**

Text files are based on posts and have access to all the same placeholders as other media **except**

Some placeholders will be changed

[Downloading Text Fileschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts/downloading-text-files)

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options/customizing-save-path#metadata)

metadata


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls where metadata is save

[Setting metadata pathchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/setting-metadata-path)

* * *

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    /home/James/Data/ofscraper/{model_username}/{responsetype}/
    {mediatype}/{filename}.{ext}

Copy

    
    {response_type}=Posts,Messages,Paid,etc
    {post_id}= ID of post
    {media_id} =ID of media
    
    {file_name} = the filename, videos wills include the quality i.e source,720
    {only_file_name}= the filename,videos will not include quality
    {original_filename}= filename as sent by onlyfans, may or may not include source
    
    {media_type}=Images,Audios,Videos
    {quality} = quality of the media, none videos will always be source
    
    {value}=The content's value: Whether it's categorized as Paid or Free.
    
    {model_id}= Unique identification number for model
    
    {first_letter}= first letter of model's username
    
    {site_name} = Onlyfans
    {text} = The text within the media. Truncation of file names has been tested to fit within OS limits, 
    still it's advisable to establish a text length limit.
    {date}= The date of the post, outputed in the config date format
    
    {model_username} = The model's username
    {username} = The model's username
    {profile} = The currently active profile
    {my_username}=The authorized account's username
    {my_id} = The identification number 
    for the  authorized account
    {label} = The label assigned to the post, if available
    {download_type}= Indication of whether it's protected or normal, 
    determined by the necessity for decryption
    
    {current_price}= Free if current price is 0 dollars else paid
    {regular_price}=Free if regular price is 0 dollars else paid
    {promo_price}= Free if promo price is 0 dollars else paid
    {renewal_price}= Free if renewal price is 0 dollars else paid
    {args}= the passed arguments namespace, keys can be access 
    with the dot (.) syntax
    {config}= the config arguments dictionary, keys can be access 
    with the [] syntax
    {modelObj} = model data class via class folder, properties can be access 
    via the dot (.) syntax
    {configPath} = path to current config directory
    

Copy

    {ext} = The file extension of the media
    

Copy

    - media_id 
    - download type

Copy

    - filename is replace with text
    - quality will always be Source
    - media_type will always be "Text"

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/scraping-individual-posts-or-media#advanced)

Advanced


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To grasp this better, checking out the `**get_info**` function in `**manual.py**` is the ideal way as it accepts a wider range of URLs.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/scraping-individual-posts-or-media#scraping-individual-media)

Scraping Individual Media


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**1\. Run a content scraper mode**

[Content Check Modeschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes)

**2\. Use the mouse to toggle the checkmark of the row you want to download** _Note you can also toggle with ";" or "',"_

Only unlocked media will have a checkmark

*   media marked for download will have 'added' in them
    

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fdatawhores%2FOF-Scraper%2Fassets%2F67020411%2F48e3badd-5502-480b-aeaa-04d58c769dd1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe68a998&sv=2)

image

**3\. Click Send to OF-Scraper**

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fdatawhores%2FOF-Scraper%2Fassets%2F67020411%2F9727c122-73ea-4043-850a-4d4fe0ffbf33&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8827ebcb&sv=2)

image

Downloads progress will be updated in console

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fdatawhores%2FOF-Scraper%2Fassets%2F67020411%2F9d0748b2-c036-4b7f-91c0-499b78a808e1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f224b020&sv=2)

image

**4\. Finished Downloads will have the words download in them**

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fdatawhores%2FOF-Scraper%2Fassets%2F67020411%2F7ae553c7-94d1-4a03-a44f-83fd056b80f9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2517cdaa&sv=2)

image

You can redownload by using ";" or "'" to untoggle and then retoggle with the added value

Status

Meaning

added

content is ready to be added to queue

downloading

content is added to queue, and will be downloaded

downloaded

content was downloaded and all post process were successful

failed

content was not downloaded and or post process failed

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/scraping-individual-posts-or-media#good-things-to-know)

Good things to know

*   Downloads won't start off immediately because the program is designed to check the queue for new downloads every 10 seconds.
    
*   Since there isn't a progress bar, enabling debug mode could be helpful in this situation.
    
*   By clicking on the table, you can instantly add more downloads. Any entry marked as "downloading" will be inaccessible for modification
    
*   Sorting and filtering functionalities should also be operational
    

[PreviousPre 3.10.7 filteringchevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes/table-management/pre-3.10.7-filtering)
[NextMetadatachevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page)

# File Output Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options#save-path-options)

Save Path Options


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Placeholderschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options/customizing-save-path)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options#save_location)

save\_location

root save folder

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options#dir_format)

dir\_format

format for directory

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options#file_format)

file\_format

format for files

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options#textlength)

textlength

Sets a cap on the text placeholder to a certain number of words, with 0 indicating an unrestricted text length

to restrict by letter count pass `--letter-count` argument

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options#space-replacer)

space-replacer

circle-info

**This change applies exclusively to the filename and doesn't affect other path components like parent directories.**

This character will replace all spaces within the filename.

It should be employed in conjunction with the text placeholder

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options#text_type_default)

text\_type\_default

Whether to count text based on words on letters

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options#truncation_default)

truncation\_default

*   If set to true text that is calculated to be over system limit will be shorted
    
*   Files whose paths are over the limit may still fail
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options#date)

date

The date syntax doesn't use bracket notation; it adheres to the Arrow implementation.

For more information, check the documentation at

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Farrow.readthedocs.io%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5c08848&sv=2)User’s Guide — Arrow 🏹 1.4.0 documentationarrow.readthedocs.iochevron-right](https://arrow.readthedocs.io/en/latest/guide.html#supported-tokens)

If you need additional help, feel free to open an issue in the repository for support.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options#other-related-options)

Other Related Options


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These options also effect the final file name

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/file-output-options#responsetype)

responsetype

# Controlling Output/Logs | OF-Scraper

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/controlling-output#log-streams)

Log Streams


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/controlling-output#discord)

Discord

circle-info

**Discord logs will solely contain the log message, whereas other logs will include additional details like function calls and line numbers.**

circle-info

**You can turn the const value 'DISCORD\_ASYNC' to true to spend up discord logs This could result in logs not being in order**

circle-info

**For optimal performance with Discord, it's recommended to use the Normal or below logging level. Levels like Debug generate a significant amount of data, requiring numerous requests to process and log**

The output goes to the Discord channel

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/controlling-output#levels)

LEVELS

_In ascending output order_

*   OFF
    
*   LOW
    
*   NORMAL
    
*   DEBUG
    
*   TRACE
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/controlling-output#output)

Output

**output to the console**

circle-info

**For clear console output, it is recommended to set the logging level to Normal or below to avoid excessive messages**

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/controlling-output#levels-1)

LEVELS

_In ascending output order_

*   PROMPT
    
*   LOW
    
*   NORMAL
    
*   DEBUG
    
*   TRACE
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/controlling-output#log)

Log

**output to logfile within the config folder**

_In ascending output order_

*   OFF
    
*   LOW
    
*   NORMAL
    
*   DEBUG
    
*   TRACE
    

Deprecated

*   STAT
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/controlling-output#log-levels-details)

Log levels details


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With the 1.9 release, you gain increased control over the output level.

**OFF**

**PROMPT**

**LOW**

**STATS**

circle-info

**Removed in 3.5**

**NORMAL**.

**DEBUG**

**TRACE**

Copy

    
    This feature allows you to deactivate Discord or log file logging. 
    By default, these outputs are turned off.

Copy

    
    The program needs prompts and specific console output for certain operations. 
    It configures console output to only show necessary information. 
    Providing a scraping action and usernames should largely disable most,
     if not all, additional output.

Copy

    
    It disables all progress bars and displays essential program status while running. 
    It also includes avatars and applies to all output destinations.

Copy

    
    Slight modification to LOW no avatars will be shown
    

Copy

    The default console output level, progress bars
     and general status messages are displayed. 
     All output destinations, including Discord and log files, 
     receive general status messages but exclude progress bars.

Copy

    It includes debugger messages and tracebacks within the 
    'Normal' output level. 
    This applies to all output destinations.
    

Copy

    
    This mode provides the most detailed and extensive 
    information compared to all other modes.

# Pre 3.10.7 filtering | OF-Scraper

circle-info

**For <3.10.7**

circle-info

**In new versions the filtering is no longer applied automatically**

circle-info

**The top bar was also replaced with a scrollable sidebar**

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fdatawhores%2FOF-Scraper%2Fassets%2F67020411%2F7aba01b5-e768-43aa-ba98-6d85aca4e37e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ca12a2d4&sv=2)

image

The form above contains all the filters. Clicking 'Submit' will apply the selected filters to the form

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes/table-management/pre-3.10.7-filtering#adding-filter-from-table)

Adding filter from table

Click on a cell to heighlight it

enter semicolon: \[ ;\] or apostrophe: \[ ' \] the table will filter to rows matching that cell value

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes/table-management/pre-3.10.7-filtering#example)

Example

The word 'videos' is highlighted

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F373772994-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FOlkVHnCqS3EnmDo4hGKm%252Fuploads%252FPSb4UwhixoFgKjTHyA0T%252Fimg1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c5e1d30-6632-4154-a605-3af513c50217&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b565baa&sv=2)

Once enter semicolon: \[ ;\] or apostrophe: \[ ' \] is pressed

only cell matching videos will appear

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fdatawhores%2FOF-Scraper%2Fassets%2F67020411%2F11911f08-2e0c-4759-b033-1fcaf40a5e6f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f9ed7afa&sv=2)

image

Furthermore, the forum will also refresh. This cycle continues until you press the reset button.
