# Old Menu | OF-Scraper

Running the prompt menu allows you to to utilize the program while passing minimal arguments

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/using-prompts/old-menu#getting-to-the-main-menu)

Getting to the main menu


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fuser-images.githubusercontent.com%2F67020411%2F230734717-e85b02ee-2e66-467a-abe0-2f479c1e6671.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aacffb42&sv=2)

image

The simplest method is to execute this command

Basically, any command lacking a scraping option will trigger the menu display

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/using-prompts/old-menu#edit-profile)

Edit Profile


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fuser-images.githubusercontent.com%2F67020411%2F230734759-b16a49da-0b61-44fc-9013-be0b0ac56419.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e37e480d&sv=2)

image

Use this option to

*   add profiles
    
*   change the default profile
    
*   rename a profile
    
*   delete profile
    

Each profile corresponds to a single account. So, if you aim to have multiple accounts, you'll require multiple profiles

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/using-prompts/old-menu#edit-config.json)

Edit config.json


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fuser-images.githubusercontent.com%2F67020411%2F230734909-5ad9c464-4984-4594-a0de-676344b84697.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e262b022&sv=2)

image

To bypass the hassle of finding the config file's location, utilize this to modify settings directly from within the script.

Your prior choices will be available, allowing you the chance to edit them conveniently.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/using-prompts/old-menu#edit-auth.json)

Edit auth.json


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**if the authentication fails, the authentication menu will pop up, prompting you to enter new settings**

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fuser-images.githubusercontent.com%2F67020411%2F230735133-9bc6c48f-daed-40be-841c-0d84c3eb2bca.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=93c6272e&sv=2)

image

Typically this is not a setting that needs to be access manually

However, you have the option to directly modify the authentication JSON using this method.

# Scripts | OF-Scraper

triangle-exclamation

All files must end with a .py to be auto-detected by OF-Scraper as a python file

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/scripts#naming-scripts)

Naming Scripts


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These scripts would be place into the naming\_script section of the config

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/scripts#rename-jpeg-to-jpg)

rename jpeg to jpg

Copy

    import sys
    import json
    import pathlib
    def main():
        input_json_str = sys.stdin.read()
    
        # 1. Parse the JSON string into a Python dictionary
        data = json.loads(input_json_str)
        #2  Fix name
        dir=data["dir"]
        file=data["file"].replace("jpeg","jpg").strip()
        filename=str(pathlib.Path(dir,file))
        #2. Print to stdout for output
        print(filename, file=sys.stdout)
        #3. Print all information data to stderr
        print(filename, file=sys.stderr)
    if __name__=="__main__":
        main()
    
    

[PreviousEnable label scanchevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/enable-label-scan)
[NextRecipeschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/recipes)

Last updated 9 months ago

# Redownload Deleted Downloads | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/recipes/redownload-deleted-downloads#with-metadata-recommended)

With metadata (recommended)


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

**make sure to use the same exact settings for both steps to make sure the same posts are being effected**

Recommended run

1.  **use the 'metadata-update' argument**
    

*   This will update files on system based on config, if a file does not exist on system it will be marked as not downloaded in data
    
*   Much faster then --dupe, since no files are writing to disk, and the number of requests required is greatly reduced
    

Copy

    ofscraper metadata --metadata-update

*   add additional args if needed for example --after 2000
    

1.  **Download normally**
    

*   If any files are missing now they will be redownloaded
    

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/recipes/redownload-deleted-downloads#force-all-downloads)

Force all downloads


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    ofscraper --force-all

this will force all downloads to be processed

[PreviousAdding Proxychevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/recipes/adding-proxy)
[NextContent Check Modeschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Creating Metadata | OF-Scraper

Metadata is automatically created when you download data. The tables and their structure are determined by the API you're using and the version of the script you're running

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/creating-metadata#metadata-mode)

metadata mode


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**you can use the --anon option to gather metadata without logging in, however this means you lose access to most media data**

metadata mode can be entered with the metadata subcommand

Copy

    ofscraper metadata [args]

This will update metadata without having to download files

[Shared Scrape and Metadata Check Mode Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options)
[Metadata Check Mode Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/metadata-check-mode-options)

[PreviousSchemachevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/schema)

# Advanced config options | OF-Scraper

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#dynamic-mode-default)

dynamic-mode-default


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   This is utilized to sign a request, essential for its authorization. Without this, the request would lack proper authorization and fail.
    
*   Generally, the options remain mostly identical. However, in rare instances, modifying these options might resolve certain issues with authentication
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#skip-unavailable-content)

skip unavailable content


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Completely bypasses the Timeline, Pinned, Archived, Labels, Stories, and Highlights API endpoints for expired users, within a specified grace period, defaults to 2 days
    
*   Continues to scan Messages, Purchased, and 'Profile' content
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#cache-mode)

cache-mode


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**You can use --no-cache**

**or --no-cache-api**

**If your having major issues with cache**

circle-info

**Options JSON SQLITE None (to disable)**

The script uses DiskCache, which has different options like SQLite and JSON.

For most folks, SQLite works fine, but if you're on a network drive, its performance might not be great. That's when switching to JSON could be a smart move, according to the author

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgrantjenks.com%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=846b6e9f&sv=2)DiskCache Tutorial — DiskCache 5.6.1 documentationgrantjenks.comchevron-right](https://grantjenks.com/docs/diskcache/tutorial.html#caveats)

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#rotate_logs)

rotate\_logs


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If set to True, each run will generate a new log. If set to False, each logs will be combined into one file per day.

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#sanitize_text)

sanitize\_text


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If set to true, text content will be sanitized before to database insertion into database

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#downloadbars)

downloadbars


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

whether to show download progress bars or not

Disabling these can improve performance

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#temp_dir)

temp\_dir


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**If not set the the final download directory is used to hold temp files**

This overrides the temporary directory used during download

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#infinite_loop_action_mode)

infinite\_loop\_action\_mode


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**You can disable the prompt for continuing the script with any arguments by setting the const value CONTINUE\_BOOL = False**

Sets the script to run in a infinite loop even when --action is used

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#logs_expire_time)

logs\_expire\_time


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Determines the maximum age for log files in hours. When log rotation is enabled, any log file older than this configured value will be automatically deleted from the system. For this feature to be active, the value must be set to a positive number greater than zero, and rotate\_logs must be enabled

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#ssl_verify)

ssl\_verify


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls how the scraper handles SSL certificate validation and TLS fingerprinting

**Available Options:**

*   `"custom"` **(Default & Recommended)** Uses a custom SSL context with TLS fingerprint hardening.
    
*   `"default"` Uses the standard Python SSL validation. This is the default behavior of the `aiohttp`
    
*   `"false"` Disables SSL certificate validation entirely
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#incremental_downloads)

incremental\_downloads


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**replaces auto\_after**

*   incrementally download content, by automatically setting --after based on successful completion of downloads in previous runs
    
    *   Deleted content is automatically detected and flagged
        
    *   ignored if --after was set by the user in the last run
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#remove_hash_match)

remove\_hash\_match


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**Set value to None to disable calculating hash, False will calculate but not remove files**

circle-info

**hashes are 128 bit and matched with file sizes to ensure uniqueness**

If at least two files with identical hashes exist on the system, remove duplicate files identified by those hashes, keeping only one copy on the file system

* * *

circle-info

**ofscraper.main or main are the default built in key words for a list combining active and expired list**

circle-info

**ofscraper.active or active are the default built in key words for active list**

circle-info

**ofscraper.expired or expired are the default built in key words for expired list**

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#default_user_list)

default\_user\_list


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**If blank then ofscraper.main is used as setting**

The default user list used during username scan

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#default_black_list)

default\_black\_list


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**If blank then the black list option is disabled**

The default black list used during username scan

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options#env_files)

env\_files


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list of files imported to set custom enviroment variables for the script

[PreviousScript Optionschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options)
[NextAuthchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/auth)

Last updated 12 days ago

# Content Check Modes | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#what-is-this)

What is this


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F373772994-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FOlkVHnCqS3EnmDo4hGKm%252Fuploads%252FZTDHos4WKp0uNHr2iHK7%252Fimage2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da777f01c-e93e-4804-b5b0-6c6660864eeb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e22160b6&sv=2)

It scrapes data from OnlyFans.com, parsing the database to showcase content information via a generated table.

Each media item occupies its own row within the table, which is searchable and offers filtering options. The table is comprehensive, containing various details for each entry

*   price of content
    
*   Will try to show if media is in your library based on media id
    
*   If the media is unlocked
    
*   The post that a media is connected
    
*   Date the media was posted
    
*   text included with the media
    
*   Length of media
    

It utilizes caching to expedite processes.

The cache is established either during regular scraping or when running in content check mode, persisting for a day before the program updates with fresh data. Additionally, you can employ '--force' to fetch the most recent information.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#cmdline-arguments)

cmdline arguments


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#undefined)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#post-check-mode)

Post Check Mode

This functionality is for reviewing posts on the main timeline or for paid content accessed through the post URL

1.  you must add the --url or --file argument
    
2.  You can combine the previous args
    
3.  \--url can be split by comma or passed multiple times
    
4.  \--file can only be passed once, and does not spit string will be interpreted as single url
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#examples)

Examples

`ofscraper post_check --url url,url,url`

`ofscraper post_check --url url --url url`

`ofscraper post_check --file file`

`ofscraper post_check --file file --url url`

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#file)

File

Should contain accepted urls line separated

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#accepted-urls)

Accepted urls

**post page**

**model page**

**model name**

**model number**

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#undefined-1)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#message-check-mode)

Message Check Mode

To avoid redundancy, the "check mode" is equivalent to "post\_check," differing only in the accepted types of posts.

When the cache expires all messages must be scraped again.

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#examples-1)

Examples

Again all the previous examples will work

`ofscraper msg_check --url url,url,url`

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#accepted-urls-1)

Accepted urls

**chat page**

**model name**

**model number**

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#undefined-2)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#paid-check-mode)

Paid Check Mode

It gathers paid content using the username provided

1.  you must add the --username or --file argument
    
2.  You can combine the previous args
    
3.  \--username can be split by comma or passed multiple times
    
4.  \--file can only be passed once, and does not spit string will be interpreted as single username
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#examples-2)

Examples

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#file-1)

File

Should contain usernames line separated

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#accepted-username)

Accepted username

**model name**

**model number**

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#undefined-3)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#story-check-mode)

Story Check Mode

It collects stories and highlights using the provided username

> stories are temporary content and may change frequently

1.  you must add the --username or --file argument
    
2.  You can combine the previous args
    
3.  \--username can be split by comma or passed multiple times
    
4.  \--file can only be passed once, and does not spit string will be interpreted as single username
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#examples-3)

Examples

`ofscraper story_check --username username,username`

`ofscraper story_check --username username --username username`

`ofscraper story_check --file file`

`ofscraper story_check --file file --username username`

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#file-2)

File

Should contain usernames line separated

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#undefined-4)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes#getting-latest-content)

Getting latest content

In each of these modes, details for each model are cached for 24 hours. To fetch the most recent content, append the "--force" argument to any of these modes.

[PreviousRedownload Deleted Downloadschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/recipes/redownload-deleted-downloads)
[NextTable Columnschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes/table-columns)

# Downloading Purchases From Deleted Models | OF-Scraper

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts/deleted-models#scrape-paid)

\--scrape-paid

This is intended for scraping paid content specifically from deleted models. The regular scraper already covers content from models with active accounts This is the only type of content that can be scraped in that case

# CDM Setup | OF-Scraper

To handle encrypted content, you'll require a CDM (Content Decryption Module). Indicators for this are the utilization of 'tempvideo' and 'tempaudio'.\\

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options#manual)

Manual

This method is recommended due to its reliability and independence from potential issues like loss of third-party access or service shutdowns.

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options#setup)

Setup

*   Follow this guide:
    

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fforum.videohelp.com%2Ffavicon-196x196.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d56626dc&sv=2)Dumping Your own L3 CDM with Android Studiowww.videohelp.comchevron-right](https://forum.videohelp.com/threads/408031-Dumping-Your-own-L3-CDM-with-Android-Studio/page26#post2766668)

Guide

*   In the end you should have two files - private key file
    
    \-client id file
    
*   Save the files to a location that is easily accessible
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options#changing-via-config-manually)

Changing via config manually

change key-mode-default

change client-id and private-key

Ensure you utilize the complete file path

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options#changing-via-the-prompt-menu)

Changing via the prompt menu

*   go to edit advance config settings menu in the prompt menu
    

chevron-rightprompt menu[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options#prompt-menu)

[https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-promptsarrow-up-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-prompts)

*   Switch to manual key-mode when prompted
    
*   When asked for the private-key, provide the complete path
    
*   When requested for the client-id, provide the complete path
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options#cdrm)

CDRM

This is the initial automated option provided by

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdrm-project.com%2Ffavico.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=428adeb2&sv=2)CDRM-Projectcdrm-project.comchevron-right](https://cdrm-project.com/)

If you're unable to access the site, it's likely down, and you'll need to choose an alternative.

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options#changing-via-config-manually-1)

Changing via config manually

change key-mode-default

you could also pass --key-mode arg

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options#changing-via-the-prompt-menu-1)

Changing via the prompt menu

*   Navigate to the "Edit Config Settings" section
    
*   Navigate to the "Edit Advanced Options" section
    
*   When prompted to choose the key-mode, opt for "cdrm".
    

[PreviousMetadata locationchevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/metadata-location)
[NextCDM issueschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options/cdm-issues)

Last updated 9 months ago

*   [Manual](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options#manual)
    
*   [CDRM](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options#cdrm)

Copy

    key-mode-default:manual

Copy

    private-key:...??privatekey.pem

Copy

    client-id:...??client_id.bin

Copy

    key-mode-default:cdrm

Copy

    --key-mode cdrm

# Testing | OF-Scraper

The repository includes a set of various tests in its suite.

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/testing#install)

Install


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tests have specific requirements and can be installed using 'poetry install --with tests'

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/testing#running)

Running


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Afterwards, you can execute the test suite using 'pytest' from the cloned repository

# Request Change to Doc | OF-Scraper

The documents are synchronized with GitHub

To propose a change, you can create a pull request at:

# Multiple Actions | OF-Scraper

circle-info

**\--post is a short hand for selecting both --like-area and --download-area**

circle-info

**\--like-area and --download area have preference over --post**

Copy

    ofscraper --action like,download --like-area pinned --download-area timeline

# Download Toggles | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options/download-toggles#auto_resume)

auto\_resume


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**replaces partfileclean**

If you set this to false, the script will delete .part files, and will not be able to auto resume

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options/download-toggles#system_free_min)

system\_free\_min


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**set to 0 to disable**

forces the script to crash if free space limit is bypassed

checked

*   Before scraping
    
*   Before each download starts

# Enable label scan | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/enable-label-scan#what-changed)

**what changed?**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Version 3.9 introduces a performance optimization to the** `**--all**` **command by streamlining label utilization**

*   In previous versions, the `--all` command relied on labels primarily to extract data and populate the labels table
    
*   While this functionality remains valuable for specific workflows, it can introduce extend scan times if you don't require labels in your database
    
*   To address this, Version 3.9 the default is to disable label usage , resulting in a performance improvement for the `--all command`
    

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/enable-label-scan#adding-labels-to-all)

adding labels to all


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    ofscraper --posts all,labels

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/enable-label-scan#scraping-just-labels)

scraping just labels


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    ofscraper --posts labels

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/enable-label-scan#shorthands-for-scraping-all-posts--labels)

shorthands for scraping all posts + labels


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    ofscraper --posts labels*

or

Copy

    ofscraper --posts labels+

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/enable-label-scan#permanently-add-labels-to-all)

permanently add labels to all


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Scripting tips | OF-Scraper

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/scripting-tips#windows)

Windows


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/scripting-tips#creating-shortcut)

creating shortcut

If you want to modify for example the binaries with additional arguments, and have these applied everytime a binary is click

1.  add arguments to the script you must first create a shortcut,
    
    \-this is because arguments can only be added to shortcuts and not the original .exe.
    
2.  create a shortcut, copy the original .exe, right click wherever you would like the shortcut to be (can be same folder) and select 'Paste shortcut' like so:
    

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F373772994-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FOlkVHnCqS3EnmDo4hGKm%252Fuploads%252FSFfBMXoFHsjdFB6rLFRK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc30a6604-a75b-4bfc-85ad-37e6ba100c6d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87d79db6&sv=2)

1.  Right click on this new shortcut, select properties and add the arguments to the end of the target field like so:
    

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F373772994-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FOlkVHnCqS3EnmDo4hGKm%252Fuploads%252F7cnRSx2MSmrPmdmUfRZ6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7242db24-0b52-4736-822a-8681e05351fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a982705&sv=2)

[PreviousAdvanced Argschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/advanced-args)
[NextEnable label scanchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/enable-label-scan)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Liking/Unliking Post | OF-Scraper

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/liking-unliking-post#liking-unliking-content)

Liking/Unliking content


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

     ofscraper --action like

Copy

     ofscraper --action unlike

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/liking-unliking-post#selecting-posts)

Selecting Posts


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/liking-unliking-post#by-post-type)

By post type

A comma-separated list indicating the posts from which you wish to download content.

Copy

     ofscraper --action like --posts pinned,timeline

multiple calls

Copy

     ofscraper --action like --posts pinned --posts timeline

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/liking-unliking-post#options)

Options

*   timeline
    
*   archived
    
*   pinned
    
*   labels
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/liking-unliking-post#special-options)

Special Options

*   all (adding this option means scraping timeline,archived,,pinned)
    
*   labels\* or labels+ (This means scraping all+labels)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/liking-unliking-post#remove-post-type)

remove post type

You can add remove a post type by prepending the type with a hyphen (-). This will override any other selection, including those from 'all'

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/liking-unliking-post#limits)

Limits


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/liking-unliking-post#onlyfans-rate-limit)

Onlyfans rate limit

estimated to be around 1000 per day

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/liking-unliking-post#limit-in-program)

Limit in program

*   Each like/unlike requests will have a delay
    
*   Which will prevent the program from just spamming likes to the onlyfans server, and prevent log outs
    
*   The limit is about a second, but is randomized
    

[PreviousBasic Actionschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions)
[NextDownloading Contentchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts)

# Table Management | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes/table-management#sorting-the-table)

Sorting the table


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the column labels on the top ![image](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fdatawhores%2FOF-Scraper%2Fassets%2F67020411%2F14ca5b89-c9c1-44bc-936e-db4683f81823&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1ace064e&sv=2)

*   First click will be desc
    
*   second click will be asc
    
*   Alternates after
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes/table-management#filtering-of-the-table)

Filtering of the table


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F373772994-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FOlkVHnCqS3EnmDo4hGKm%252Fuploads%252FuARoi3HxLPRQLOtakPOD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfdbc411c-db14-4af4-889d-b371726cfd73&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b02743c&sv=2)

*   Toggle the form with Ctrl+S
    
*   The filter form contains fields for all the columns in the table.
    
*   Clicking 'Filter' applies form values to filter the table.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes/table-management#adding-value-from-table)

Adding value from table

*   Click on a cell to heighlight it
    
*   enter semicolon: \[ ;\] or apostrophe: \[ ' \]
    
*   the matching field in the filter form, will use the value from the cell
    
*   To apply click 'Filter'
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes/table-management#example)

Example

The table a cell with the word 'videos' is highlighted in the mediatype column

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F373772994-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FOlkVHnCqS3EnmDo4hGKm%252Fuploads%252FPSb4UwhixoFgKjTHyA0T%252Fimg1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c5e1d30-6632-4154-a605-3af513c50217&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b565baa&sv=2)

Pressing semicolon (`;`) or apostrophe (\`) confirms your choice and updates the filter form

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F373772994-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FOlkVHnCqS3EnmDo4hGKm%252Fuploads%252F5YdQCDXIxG1U7wNJKe7f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dddf19d5e-e88b-45d2-9f38-bf256cb3ba9d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c22a44be&sv=2)

Clicking "Filter" applies the changes, showing only videos in the table.

![](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fdatawhores%2FOF-Scraper%2Fassets%2F67020411%2F11911f08-2e0c-4759-b033-1fcaf40a5e6f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f9ed7afa&sv=2)

image

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes/table-management#undefined)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/content-check-modes/table-management#reset-the-table)

Reset the table

Click on the reset button. Keep in mind, the program saves the current table information in memory, so it won't fetch new data until you restart it

###

# Basic Automation with command-line | OF-Scraper

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions#basic-run)

Basic Run


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This enables you to choose arguments using the prompt menus.

Copy

    ofscraper

[Downloading Contentchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts)
[Model Filtering/Sortingchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting)
[Liking/Unliking Postchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/liking-unliking-post)

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions#performing-action-s)

Performing action(s)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**\--post is a short hand used for all actions unless an --like-area or --download-area command is passed**

You can combine these actions together

*   likes or unlike (only 1 because liking and unliking all posts doesn't make sense)
    
*   combine the previous with download
    

This command will download all wall posts for the selected model and simultaneously like all the posts

Copy

     ofscraper --posts all --action like,download

This command will only download

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions#selecting-different-areas)

Selecting different areas

You can use

*   like-area specifically for like/unlike action
    
*   download-area specifically for the download action
    

This command will download all post, but only like pinned

or

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions#bypass-all-prompts)

Bypass all prompts


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**You must pick timeline,pinned, or archived to bypass the like area prompt when doing action**

**like or unlike**

To bypass prompts

*   Select at least one scraping method
    
*   Provide a username(s)
    
*   Providing the areas to scan
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions#running-command-in-the-background)

Running command in the background


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For daemon mode to function, you must select at least one scraping method

circle-info

**In daemon mode, if the --username argument isn't provided, it will prompt you to pick a username only once**

circle-info

**In daemon mode, if the --post or --scrape-paid argument isn't provided, it will prompt you to them only once**

The script will operate at least every 10 minutes. If a run extends beyond 10 minutes, the subsequent run begins immediately after the prior one concludes.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions#modifications-to-filename)

Modifications to Filename


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions#toggle-letter-count-for-textlength)

Toggle letter count for textlength

By default, 'textlength' corresponds to the maximum number of words you desire. To modify this to represent the maximum number of letters, use the '--letter-count' argument.

# Price Filtering/Sort | OF-Scraper

circle-exclamation

**Fallbacks are to utilized to enable easy sorting of list**

circle-exclamation

**Fallbacks can be eliminated with proper filtering**

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort#current-price)

Current Price


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**Best used with --active-subscription**

1.  If there is an active subscription and its subscription price is available, use that price.
    
2.  If there is no active subscription or the subscription price is not available, check for active promotions with a "claimable" tag. Use the lowest subscription price among these promotions.
    
3.  If no "claimable" promotions are available, use the regular subscription price.
    
4.  If none of the above methods provide a valid price, then 0 is used as a fallback
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort#renewal-price)

_Renewal Price_


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**Best used with --active-subscription**

1.  Primary Source is the lowest claimable promotional subscription price.
    
2.  If no "claimable" promotions are available, use the regular subscription price.
    
3.  If none of the above methods provide a valid price, then 0 is used as a fallback
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort#regular-price)

Regular Price


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Primary Source is the regular subscription price.
    
2.  If that is not available then, then 0 is used as a fallback
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort#promo-price)

Promo Price


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**Best used with --promo-only or --all-promo-only**

1.  Primary Source is the lowest promotional subscription price.
    
2.  If no promotions are available, use the regular subscription price.
    
3.  If none of the above methods provide a valid price, then 0 is used as a fallback
    

[PreviousModel Filtering/Sortingchevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting)
[NextAdvanced Argschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/advanced-args)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [Current Price](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort#current-price)
    
*   [Renewal Price](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort#renewal-price)
    
*   [Regular Price](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort#regular-price)
    
*   [Promo Price](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort#promo-price)

# Schema | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/schema#schemas)

Schemas


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The schema may be extended in future versions, but existing columns will remain for backwards compatibility.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/schema#labels)

Labels

*   **id:** INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
    
*   **label\_id:** INTEGER
    
*   **name:** VARCHAR
    
*   **type:** VARCHAR
    
*   **post\_id:** INTEGER
    
*   **model\_id:** INTEGER
    
*   **UNIQUE (post\_id, label\_id, model\_id)**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/schema#medias)

Medias

*   **model\_id**: INTEGER
    
*   **hash**: VARCHAR
    
*   **unlocked**: BOOL
    
*   **duration**: VARCHAR
    
*   **posted\_at**: TIMESTAMP
    
*   **created\_at**: TIMESTAMP
    
*   **downloaded**: BOOL
    
*   **linked**: BOOL
    
*   **preview**: INTEGER
    
*   **media\_type**: VARCHAR
    
*   **api\_type**: VARCHAR
    
*   **size**: INTEGER
    
*   **filename**: VARCHAR
    
*   **directory**: VARCHAR
    
*   **link**: VARCHAR
    
*   **post\_id**: INTEGER NOT NULL
    
*   **media\_id**: INTEGER
    
*   **id**: INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
    
*   **UNIQUE (media\_id, model\_id, post\_id)**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/schema#messages)

Messages

*   **model\_id:** INTEGER
    
*   **user\_id:** INTEGER
    
*   **created\_at:** TIMESTAMP
    
*   **archived:** BOOLEAN
    
*   **paid:** BOOLEAN
    
*   **price:** INTEGER
    
*   **text:** VARCHAR
    
*   **post\_id:** INTEGER NOT NULL
    
*   **id:** INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
    
*   **UNIQUE (post\_id, model\_id)**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/schema#posts)

**Posts**

*   **model\_id:** INTEGER
    
*   **created\_at** :TIMESTAMP
    
*   **opened:** BOOLEAN
    
*   **stream:** BOOLEAN
    
*   **pinned:** BOOLEAN
    
*   **archived:** BOOLEAN
    
*   **paid:** INTEGER
    
*   **price:** INTEGER
    
*   **text:** VARCHAR
    
*   **post\_id:** INTEGER NOT NULL
    
*   **id:** INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
    
*   **UNIQUE** (**post\_id**, **model\_id**)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/schema#stories)

Stories

*   **model\_id:** INTEGER
    
*   **created\_at:** TIMESTAMP
    
*   **archived:** BOOLEAN
    
*   **paid:** INTEGER
    
*   **price:** INTEGER
    
*   **text:** VARCHAR
    
*   **post\_id:** INTEGER NOT NULL
    
*   **id:** INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
    
*   **UNIQUE (post\_id, model\_id)**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/schema#models)

Models

*   **id:** INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
    
*   **model\_id:** INTEGER NOT NULL
    
*   **UNIQUE model\_id**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/schema#profiles)

Profiles

*   **username**: VARCHAR NOT NULL
    
*   **user\_id**: INTEGER NOT NULL
    
*   **id**: INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
    
*   **UNIQUE (user\_id, username)**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/schema#products)

Products

*   **id**: INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
    
*   **post\_id**: INTEGER NOT NULL
    
*   **model\_id**: INTEGER
    
*   **title**: VARCHAR
    
*   **created\_at**: TIMESTAMP
    
*   **archived**: BOOLEAN
    
*   **paid**: INTEGER
    
*   **price**: INTEGER
    
*   **text**: VARCHAR
    
*   **UNIQUE (post\_id, model\_id)**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/schema#others)

Others

*   `**id**`: INTEGER, NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY
    
*   `**post_id**`: INTEGER, NOT NULL
    
*   `**text**`**:** VARCHAR
    
*   `**price**`**:** INTEGER
    
*   `**paid**`**:** INTEGER
    
*   `**archived**`**:** BOOLEAN
    
*   `**created_at**`**:** TIMESTAMP
    
*   `**model_id**`**:** INTEGER
    
*   **UNIQUE (post\_id, model)**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/page/schema#schema_flags)

**Schema\_flags**

*   **flag\_name:** TEXT PRIMARY KEY
    
*   **flag\_value:** TEXT

# Downloading Text Files | OF-Scraper

circle-info

**Text files must be handled differently since there are no text media uploads; instead, they are based on the posts and tied to multiple media**

1.  **Download Text only**
    

*   Set the mediatype to only text via the --mediatypes arg or config file
    
*   This will work in download and manual,content check mode as well, It will not work in like/unlike mode
    

1.  **Download Text with other media**
    

*   Set the mediatype to include text via the --mediatypes arg or config file
    
*   Again This will work in download and manual,content check mode as well, It will not work in like/unlike mode
    

[PreviousDownloading Contentchevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts)
[NextDownloading Purchases From Deleted Modelschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts/deleted-models)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Values to Pick | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options/values-to-pick#note-on-values-to-pick)

Note on values to pick


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options/values-to-pick#threads)

Threads

*   It's recommended to use **0 to 3 threads** for downloads.
    
    *   **0 threads** means downloads will occur on the main program thread.
        
    
*   Using a combination of console debug (or higher log levels) and download progress bars might benefit from more threads.
    
*   However, in newer versions, the performance difference between different thread counts is usually minimal or non-existent.
    
*   It is recommended to log trace level to log file instead of adding more threads with console output
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options/values-to-pick#sems)

Sems

*   It's recommended to limit total downloads across all threads to **around 15**
    
*   This translates to **5 sems** if using 3 threads.
    

[PreviousPerformance Optionschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options)
[NextScript Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options)

# Advanced Download Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/download-options/advanced-download-options#backend)

backend


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Both aio and httpx can handle downloads and requests. Normally aio is faster,so switching is only required if your having issues

Historically, this has mostly been the case Mac users, and even then, only a small group among them

downloadbars


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

whether to show download progress bars or not

Disabling these can improve performance

temp\_dir


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This overrides the temporary directory used during download

# Advanced Args | OF-Scraper

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/advanced-args#profile)

\--profile

You can combine this with **'--config'**.

This option holds precedence over the currently active profile within the configuration file

Copy

    Change location of profile 

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/advanced-args#users-first)

\--users-first

This adjustment alters the download order to prioritize fetching links for all selected users initially. While this may lead to a longer wait for downloads to commence, it can prove beneficial in specific scenarios.

Copy

    ofscraper --user-first

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/advanced-args#multiple-configs)

multiple configs

Copy

    ofscraper --config folder or file

The program attempts to intelligently guess the location of your config folder.

You can observe the locations it's scanning in the table. The checks will cease upon reaching a successful match (True) or reaching the failback check.

Check

config file if True

config folder if True

\--config is not passed

$HOME/.config/ofscraper/config.json

$HOME/.config/ofscraper/

config\_arg is an existing file

config\_arg

config\_arg parentdir

config arg is an existing dir

config\_arg/config.json

config\_arg

config arg has no extension

config\_arg/config.json

config\_arg

config\_arg ends is just a single file

i.e

test.json

$HOME/.config/ofscraper/config\_arg

$HOME/.config/ofscraper

Failback always true Note: The only option is for config\_arg to be something like /home/me/test.json

config\_arg

config\_arg parentdir

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/advanced-args#shared-information)

Shared information

Two configs within the same folder can share

*   Profiles
    
*   log files
    
*   cache
    
*   authorization
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/advanced-args#duplication-check)

Duplication check

This relies on your configuration settings. If two configurations share identical metadata settings, duplicates won't exist between those configurations.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/advanced-args#multiple-profile-auth)

multiple profile auth

Authentication for various accounts is managed via profiles. You can modify the default profile either through the configuration or by using the '--profile' argument.

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/advanced-args#example)

Example

The profile is consistently located within the parent folder of the configuration file and is always appended with '\_profile'.

Hence, in this scenario, the profile would be

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/advanced-args#no-cache)

\--no-cache

Disables all caching mechanisms and removes retrieval of past data for all data

As a result, synchronous processing is enforced for APIs to ensure each request is completed before the next one begins, since processing multiple API requests concurrently relies on past data This will also disable the use of cache to speed up decryption key retrieval

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/advanced-args#no-api-cache)

\-no-api-cache

Similar to --no-cache, but only disables caching mechanisms and removes retrieval of past data for API use only

As a result, synchronous processing is enforced for APIs to ensure each request is completed before the next one begins, since processing multiple API requests concurrently relies on past data.

[PreviousPrice Filtering/Sortchevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort)
[NextScripting tipschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/scripting-tips)

# Performance Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options#thread_count)

thread\_count


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The count of threads or workers designated for downloading

Copy

    min=0
    max=system

0 threads: This is a special setting indicating that you want to use the main program thread for downloading as well

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options#caveats)

Caveats

*   It's important to note that if the thread count exceeds 0 but the number of downloads for a model doesn't equal or surpass 5 downloads per thread, only the main thread will handle the downloading process.
    
*   Additionally, the maximum number of usable threads is determined by your system, irrespective of the configuration file settings.
    
    *   on Windows and Linux The number of unused threads is provided.
        
    *   However, on Mac, the operating system lacks this specific OS API, so the maximum is established as the total number of threads on the system
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options#download-sems)

download-sems


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Max concurrent number of downloads per thread

If threads is the number of workers for downloading, then download-sems is the number of tasks each worker can process at a time

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options#download_limit)

download\_limit


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Maximum download speed per second for each thread

**Accepts**

*   human readable inputs
    
*   int representing the number of bytes per second
    

[PreviousCDM Optionschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/key-option)
[NextValues to Pickchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options/values-to-pick)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [thread\_count](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options#thread_count)
    
*   [Caveats](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options#caveats)
    
*   [download-sems](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options#download-sems)

# FAQ/Common Issues | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-1.-missing-post)

1\. Missing Post


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Certain models delete content, which restricts OF-Scraper from accessing this specific content.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-2.-number-of-users-doesnt-match-account-number)

2. Number of users doesn't match account number


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Ffluidicon.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc891f14&sv=2)429 and model missing · Issue #224 · datawhores/OF-ScraperGitHubchevron-right](https://github.com/datawhores/OF-Scraper/issues/224#issuecomment-1757367312)

Every time you scroll down, the API requests 10 names, but frequently, fewer than 10 names are returned

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#example)

Example

Account: 400 total subs

**Active Accounts**

This figure is expected to be more accurate, but it seems to update according to a schedule, so it might be slightly off until synchronization occurs.

**Expired and ALL**

The count here can be significantly impacted by expired subscriptions.

For instance, an account may indicate it has 400 subscribers, but as OnlyFans iterates through each offset \[0, 10, 20, 30,...390\], some offsets won't return 10 numbers, ultimately reducing the final count.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-3.-missing-models)

3\. Missing Models


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before creating an issue, ensure that you're using the latest version available.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-4.-lots-of-tempvideo-or-tempaudio-files)

4. Lots of tempvideo or tempaudio files


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Ensure your CDM (Content Decryption Module) is set up correctly

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fof-scraper.gitbook.io%2Fof-scraper%2F%7Egitbook%2Ficon%3Fsize%3Dsmall%26theme%3Dlight&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff8d559f&sv=2)CDM Setup | OF-Scraperof-scraper.gitbook.iochevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/cdm-options)

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-5.-something-is-not-working)

5. Something is not working


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Run the command to display the output in the console

Alternatively, run the command to output to your configuration folder.

Send the logs to a Discord channel or create a GitHub issue

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-6.-mp4decrypt-and-ffmpeg)

6\. MP4Decrypt and FFMPEG


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The mentioned programs below are necessary for downloading content, and they are compatible across various platforms.

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fffmpeg.org%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1e877ce&sv=2)Download FFmpegffmpeg.orgchevron-right](https://ffmpeg.org/download.html)

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bento4.com%2Fimages%2Ffavicon.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4529379a&sv=2)mp4decrypt - Bento4www.bento4.comchevron-right](https://www.bento4.com/documentation/mp4decrypt/)

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#binaries)

Binaries

circle-info

**If manually downloading simply provide OF-Scraper with the full path to the program in the configuration file**

[Binaries Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/binaries-options)
chevron-rightCopying path on windows [hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#copying-path-on-windows)

You can use the following software if windows does not provide an easy way to do this

[https://pathcopycopy.github.io/arrow-up-right](https://pathcopycopy.github.io/)

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-7.-ofscraper-not-found)

7. ofscraper not found


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This generally means that you need to update your PATH

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-8.-can-this-download-locked-content)

8\. Can this download locked content


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Yes.....if it was unlocked before.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-9.-status-down)

9. Status Down


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This usually indicates that your authentication information is incorrect, or you've been signed out from OnlyFans

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-10.-404-response)

10. 404 Response


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This could imply that the content you're attempting to scrape is no longer available. It might also signal that the model has deleted her account, making it inaccessible on the platform.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-11.-request-taking-a-long-time)

11. Request taking a long time


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If a request fails, OF-Scraper will pause and make several retry attempts. Frequent retries could extend the duration of certain runs.

circle-info

**Version 3.7 has a built in timelimit on requests to prevent them for being stuck forever However you can change the const value to adjust these values to your need**

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-12.-429-response)

12\. 429 Response


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   This error may stem from excessive requests, particularly when auto-liking/unliking.
    
*   The maximum appears to be 1000 per day.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-13.-409-response)

13\. 409 Response


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You might observe cases where content is unavailable on the OnlyFans site, often indicated by placeholders or non-loading media.

VPN users might experience this based on the VPN server they're connected to. Consequently, this also affects the API and OF-Scraper's ability to scrape content.

The most effective solution would be to switch VPN servers or allow some time for the situation to reset.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-14.-scrape-entire-paid-page-or-scape-paid-should-i-do-it)

14. Scrape entire paid page or --scape-paid should I do it


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The amount of content you've purchased largely determines this

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#does-the-regular-scraper-get-purchased-content)

Does the regular scraper get purchased content?

Yes, if you've chosen "purchased," all purchased content for the selected models will be scraped. This is accomplished by using the models' usernames as input on the purchase page.

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#then-why-the-prompt)

Then why the prompt

Certain models may have deleted accounts, making it necessary to scan the entire purchase page to access their purchases. Since they lack a name to use as input, a thorough scan becomes necessary.

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#when-would-you-use-to-use-it)

When would you use to use it

Personally, I rarely use this setting. However, if your scans are infrequent, it might be a good idea to turn it on.

I'd also recommend using it during your initial scan.

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#when-would-you-not-use-it)

When would you not use it

If you're conducting frequent scans, such as one per day, it's alright to turn it off for most scans

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#id-15.-ffmpeg-shared-library-not-found-error)

15\. FFmpeg shared library not found Error


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Example: : version \`GLIBCXX\_3.4.29' not found

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#cause)

Cause

Missing shared libraries

This issue appears to only affect Linux systems

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#fix)

Fix

Obtain the GPL non-shared release version.

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Ffluidicon.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc891f14&sv=2)Releases · BtbN/FFmpeg-BuildsGitHubchevron-right](https://github.com/BtbN/FFmpeg-Builds/releases)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/faq#some-info)

Some Info

*   [https://superuser.com/questions/1712179/which-version-of-ffmpeg-is-the-latestarrow-up-right](https://superuser.com/questions/1712179/which-version-of-ffmpeg-is-the-latest)
    
*   using the version in your Linux Repo may not work
