# Model Filtering/Sorting | OF-Scraper

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#filter-sort-list-by-price)

Filter/Sort List By Price


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Price Filtering/Sortchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort)

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#selecting-specific-models-from-command-line)

Selecting Specific models from command-line


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can provide a comma-separated list indicating the models you wish to scrape

Copy

     ofscraper --username name1,name

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#selecting-all-users)

Selecting all users

Copy

     ofscraper --username ALL

'ALL' is influenced by filters, and it is case-sensitive.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#filtering-username-list)

Filtering username list


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following settings can be dynamically modified if using prompts.

[Using Promptschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/using-prompts)

Furthermore, this adjustment doesn't alter the retrieval of usernames; it solely impacts the subset of usernames that are displayed

> If you wish to retrieve specific usernames, set up a collection on OnlyFans, then utilize the '--userlist' or '--blacklist' arguments accordingly

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#version-greater-than-2.1)

Version >2.1

Now, '--username' takes precedence over any filters. Consequently, only the selected '--usernames' will be utilized, with the exception of 'ALL', which can still be filtered.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#restrict-by-account-type)

Restrict by account type

This will limit the program to exclusively interact with and display free accounts

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#restrict-by-subscription-status)

Restrict by subscription status

This demonstrates scraping messages from subscriptions that have expired

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#restrict-by-renewal-status)

Restrict by renewal status

You can utilize this option to exclusively scrape active accounts, considering the renewal status of their subscriptions.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#combining-filters)

Combining filters

Filters are commonly employed to scrape accounts that are scheduled for expiration.

Alternatively, you might choose to scrape only free accounts with active subscriptions

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#exclude-specific-models)

Exclude specific models

Please note that this takes precedence over '--username', including '--username ALL'

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#filter-by-regular-price)

Filter by regular price

[Price Filtering/Sortchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#advanced-filtering)

Advanced filtering

[User List Filter Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args)

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#sorting-username-list)

Sorting username list


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The default setting is to sort alphabetically by name in ascending order

> Sorting effects the order of scraping, and not just the order that they appear in the prompt menu

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#sort-by-account-expiring-date)

sort by account expiring date

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#sort-by-account-subscribed-date)

sort by account subscribed date

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#sort-by-account-name)

sort by account name

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#sort-by-promotional-prices)

sort by promotional prices

[Price Filtering/Sortchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#desc-option)

desc option

By default, the sorting is in ascending order.

Utilizing this changes the sorting to descending order.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#retrieving-specific-list)

Retrieving specific list


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This option enables switching from the primary list of OnlyFans accounts to a previously designated collection of accounts.

You have the ability to merge multiple lists

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting#blocking-list-of-names)

Blocking list of Names


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Collections offer the functionality to block a list of names

> Please note that this takes precedence over the '--userlist' option and also 'ALL' parameter

# Downloading Content | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#selecting-posts)

Selecting Posts


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#by-post-type)

By post type

A comma-separated list indicating the posts from which you wish to download content.

Copy

     ofscraper --action download --posts highlights,timeline

multiple calls

Copy

     ofscraper --action download --posts highlights --posts timeline

Duplicates will be removed

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#options)

Options

*   profile
    
*   highlights
    
*   timeline
    
*   archived
    
*   stories
    
*   messages
    
*   purchased
    
*   pinned
    
*   labels
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#special-options)

Special Options

*   all (adding this option means scraping highlights,timeline,archived,stories,pinned,purchased and messages)
    
*   labels\* or labels+ (This means scraping all+labels)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#remove-post-type)

remove post type

You can add remove a post type by prepending the type with a hyphen (-). This will remove any selection, including those from all

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#bypass-dupe-check)

Bypass dupe check


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, content is stored in a database to prevent duplicate downloads. If you wish to download all available content for the current model, include the '--force-all' argument.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#filter-post-by-date)

Filter Post by Date


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**x should be a valid date**

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#before)

Before

Filters posts on or before the specified date. It functions for downloading, liking, and unliking posts.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#after)

After

Filter posts on or after the specified date. It functions for downloading, liking, and unliking posts.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#valid-inputs)

**Valid Inputs**

circle-info

**Read arrow documentation/repo for all valid inputs**

`YYYY-MM-DD, YYYY-M-DD, YYYY-M-D, YYYY/MM/DD, YYYY/M/DD, YYYY/M/D, YYYY.MM.DD, YYYY.M.DD, YYYY.M.D, YYYYMMDD, YYYY-DDDD, YYYYDDDD, YYYY-MM, YYYY/MM, YYYY.MM, YYYY`

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#dehumanize-strings)

Dehumanize Strings

We can convert certain strings into dates. The general rules seem to be (number) (timeframe) (ago)

**timeframes**

*   week
    
*   month
    
*   year
    
*   second
    
*   day
    

You can enhance granularity by including a comma. When utilizing debuggers, the output will display in UTC, offering greater detail.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#filtering-timed-post-promotional)

Filtering Timed Post (Promotional)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

skip all timed post

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#filtering-by-text-content)

Filtering by text content

This feature can accept regex patterns, but you might need to enclose the string in quotes to escape the input properly. Additionally, using a capital letter will initiate a case-sensitive search.

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#filter)

Filter

This will include only post that match the provided regex pattern

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#neg-filter)

Neg Filter:

This will exclude any posts that match the provided regex pattern.

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/basic-actions/selecting-posts#search-entire-paid-page)

Search entire paid page


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To exclusively scrape the paid page and skip other prompts

# Filename Modification Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/filename-modification-options#filename-modification-parameters)

Filename Modification Parameters


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/filename-modification-options#g-original)

\-g, --original

*   **Disables:** Truncation of long file paths.
    
*   **Default:** `None` (paths are truncated by default)
    
*   **Use case:** You might want to use this option if you need to preserve the entire original file path for organizational purposes.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/filename-modification-options#tt-text-type-argument)

\-tt, --text-type \[argument\]

*   **Sets:** The type of unit used to determine the maximum length of the filename text placeholder
    
*   **Possible choices:**
    
    *   `word`: (default) Splits the filename text placeholder into words and considers word count for truncation.
        
    *   `letter`: Considers the total number of characters in the filename text placeholder for truncation.
        
    
*   **Example:** With `-tt letter` and `-tl 10`, text placeholder would be truncated to a maximum of 10 characters
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/filename-modification-options#sr-space-replacer-argument-optional)

\-sr, --space-replacer \[argument\] (optional)

*   **Replaces:** Spaces in the filename text with the specified character.
    
*   **Default:** `None` (spaces are left as spaces)
    
*   **Use case:** This can be helpful for creating filenames compatible with certain file systems or applications that disallow spaces.
    
*   **Example:** With `-sr _`, spaces would be replaced with underscores (e.g., "This File.txt" becomes "This\_File.txt").
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/filename-modification-options#tl-textlength-argument)

\-tl, --textlength \[argument\]

*   **Sets:** The maximum length of the filename text placeholder
    
*   **Default:** `None` (no limit on text length)
    
*   **Effect:** Truncates text placeholders that exceed the specified length.
    
*   **Use case:** This is useful for ensuring filenames adhere to character limitations imposed by some file systems, as text placeholders can easily go over OS limits
    

**Note:**

*   These options work together to modify the final filename.
    
*   If truncation occurs, it will be based on the chosen `-tt` type (word or letter) ,the provided `-tl` length, and the current OS
    

[PreviousLogging Optionschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/logging)
[NextMedia Filters Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Filename Modification Parameters](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/filename-modification-options#filename-modification-parameters)
    
*   [\-g, --original](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/filename-modification-options#g-original)
    
*   [\-tt, --text-type \[argument\]](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/filename-modification-options#tt-text-type-argument)
    
*   [\-sr, --space-replacer \[argument\] (optional)](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/filename-modification-options#sr-space-replacer-argument-optional)
    
*   [\-tl, --textlength \[argument\]](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/filename-modification-options#tl-textlength-argument)

# Script Options | OF-Scraper

[Scriptschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/scripts)

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#post-action-script-post_download_script)

Post Action Script (`post_download_script`)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A script that runs after an action for a user has completed. This script can be configured via the `--after-action-script` command-line argument or the `after_action_script` setting in the program's configuration.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#trigger-conditions)

**Trigger Conditions**

*   Runs after each model is downloaded in the main scraper
    
    *   Including in daemon-mode
        
    
*   Runs after each model like/unlike process is finished
    
    *   Including in daemon-mode
        
    
*   Runs after each model's metadata is processed in metadata mode.
    
*   Runs after each model is processed in manual mode
    
*   Runs for each unique model, after the current cart is downloaded in check mode
    
*   Runs for each model after scrape paid is process,
    
    *   Note: modeldeleted or models without a active account would be ran together as one unit
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#data-sent)

**Data Sent**

As a JSON dictionary, typically via standard input (stdin).

*   `username`: username (string)
    
*   `action` : action ran (string)
    
*   `model_id`: model\_id (integer).
    
*   `media`: media dictionary from API, with `final_path` added, and whether they were downloaded or not
    
*   `posts`: posts dictionary from API.
    
*   `userdata`: a dictionary from the users API.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#post-script-post_script)

Post Script (`post_script`)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A script that runs after all actions for all users have completed. This script can be configured via the `--post-script` command-line argument or the `post_script` setting in the program's configuration.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#trigger-conditions-1)

**Trigger Conditions**

*   Once all models are downloaded or liked in scrape mode
    
*   After each cycle in daemon mode
    
*   Once all the posts from manual mode are completed
    
*   After the current cart downloads are processed in check mode, and after the download\_action\_script is processed for each user.
    
*   After all metadata for all users is processed in metadata mode.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#data-sent-1)

**Data Sent**

As a JSON dictionary, typically via standard input (stdin).

*   `like_processed`: A list of users who have successfully completed the 'like' action.
    
*   `like_unprocessed`: A list of users who are queued for the 'like' action but were not processed.
    
*   `unlike_processed`: A list of users who have successfully completed the 'unlike' action.
    
*   `unlike_unprocessed`: A list of users who are queued for the 'unlike' action but were not processed.
    
*   `download_processed`: A list of users whose content has been successfully downloaded.
    
*   `download_unprocessed`: A list of users whose content is queued for download but were not processed.
    
*   `scrape_paid_processed`: A list of users who were successfully processed during the 'scrape\_paid' action
    
*   `scrape_paid_unprocessed`: A list of users who are queued for the 'scrape\_paid' scrape action but but were not processed.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#naming-script-naming_script)

Naming Script (`naming_script`)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A script that dynamically generates the final filename or full path for a downloaded media item. This script can be configured via the `--naming-script` command-line argument or the `naming_script` setting in the program's configuration.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#trigger-conditions-2)

**Trigger Conditions**

*   For each individual media item, this script runs while its temporary filename is being generated.
    
*   It is executed again after the temporary file has been downloaded, and before the file is renamed to its final destination.
    
*   **As a special case, the script also runs before generating filenames for text files when using the** `**--text**` **or** `**--text-only**` **option.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#data-sent-2)

**Data Sent**

As a JSON dictionary, typically via standard input (stdin)

*   `media`: A dictionary representing the media item
    
*   `post`: The dictionary representing the post associated with the media item.
    
*   `dir`: The calculated directory path (string).
    
*   `file`: The calculated filename (string).
    
*   `dir_format`: The current directory format string (string from config).
    
*   `file_format`: The current file format string (string from config).
    
*   `metadata`: The current metadata format setting (string from config).
    
*   `username`: The model's username (string).
    
*   `model_id`: The model's ID (integer).
    
*   `post_id`: The ID of the post associated with the media (integer).
    
*   `media_id`: The ID of the media item (integer).
    
*   `media_type`: The type of media
    
*   `value`: The value associated with the media
    
*   `date`: The formatted date related to the media/post (string)
    
*   `response_type`: The response type of the media (string).
    
*   `label`: A string representing associated labels
    
*   `download_type`: The type of download
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#expected-output)

**Expected Output**

The script is expected to print the desired the **full desired path** to standard output (stdout). The scraper will then use this output to rename or move the downloaded file

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#after-download-script-download_skip_script)

After Download Script (`download_skip_script`)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A script that runs after a download has completed. This script can be configured via the `--after-download-script` command-line argument or the `after_download_script` setting in the program's configuration.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#trigger-conditions-3)

**Trigger Conditions**

*   It executes after a download has successfully been downloaded
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#data-sent-3)

**Data Sent**

a single string

*   The final filepath of the download
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#download-skip-script-download_skip_script)

Download Skip Script (`download_skip_script`)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A script that determines whether to skip or continue a download. This script can be configured via the `--download-skip-script` command-line argument or the `download_skip_script` setting in the program's configuration.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#trigger-conditions-4)

**Trigger Conditions**

*   It executes before the download process begins for each individual media item.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#data-sent-4)

**Data Sent**

As a JSON dictionary, typically via standard input (stdin).

*   `username`: The model's username (string).
    
*   `model_id`: The model's ID (integer).
    
*   `post_id`: The ID of the post associated with the media (integer).
    
*   `media_id`: The ID of the media item (integer).
    
*   `media`: dictionary representing the media item to be downloaded.
    
*   `post`: A dictionary representing the post associated with the media item.
    
*   `total_size`: The total size of the download in bytes (integer).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options#expected-output-1)

**Expected Output**

The script is expected to return a string via standard output (stdout).

*   If the returned string is `"False"` (case-insensitive) or an empty string, the download will be **skipped**.
    
*   Any other non-empty string returned will allow the download to **proceed**.

[NextAdvanced config optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/advanced-config-options)

# Metadata Check Mode Options | OF-Scraper

circle-info

**Metadata Mode inherits mosts options from the main/scraper mode, with a few options removed because they don't make sense outside of downloading**

* * *

circle-info

**without --force-all or --force-model-unique media will be filter to only those that are set as not downloaded in the database**

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/metadata-check-mode-options#syntax)

Syntax


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    ofscraper metadata [options]

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/metadata-check-mode-options#example)

example

Copy

    ofscraper metadata -metadata check

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/metadata-check-mode-options#general-options)

General Options


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[General Program Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups)
[Shared Scrape and Metadata Check Mode Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options)

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/metadata-check-mode-options#options)

Options


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/metadata-check-mode-options#md-metadata-argument)

\-md, --metadata \[argument\]

The `--metadata` argument is used to specify how metadata mode updates the db

**Available Modes:**

*   **check** - Updates metadata fields for the specified area via an API. This option does not check for new filenames.
    
*   **update** - This mode performs two actions:
    
    1.  Updates download status and filenames based on the presence of actual files.
        
    2.  Updates metadata fields for the specified area via an API.
        
    
*   **complete** - Marks the download as complete and updates metadata fields via an API. It also uses a new filename if one is available
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/metadata-check-mode-options#ms-mark-stray-locked-argument)

\-ms, --mark-stray-locked \[argument\]

Marks unmatched media items as locked.

**Details:**

*   This flag is designed to identify and manage media items retrieved using the `--after` and `--before` options (date range filtering) that cannot be retrieved again through the API (potentially due to deletion).
    
*   Media items with labels are excluded from being marked as locked.
    
*   Locking is applied on a per-API type basis, Timeline, Archived Posts, and Messages
    
*   This has no effect if --scrape-paid is the only argument
    

**Use Case:**

Use this option to manage media items that aren't retrievable via the APIs. Marking them as locked prevents main scraper from using these items to set the minimum date

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/metadata-check-mode-options#sp-scrape-paid-argument)

\-sp, --scrape-paid \[argument\]

The `--scrape-paid` argument is used to specify how metadata mode updates the db, for scrape paid content

The options are the same as --metadata

*   **check** - Updates metadata fields for the specified area via an API. This option does not check for new filenames.
    
*   **update** - This mode performs two actions:
    
    1.  Updates download status and filenames based on the presence of actual files.
        
    2.  Updates metadata fields for the specified area via an API.
        
    
*   **complete** - Marks the download as complete and updates metadata fields via an API. It also uses a new filename if one is available
    

**Available Modes:**

*   **check** - Updates metadata fields for the specified area via an API. This option does not check for new filenames.
    
*   **update** - This mode performs two actions:
    
    1.  Updates download status and filenames based on the presence of actual files.
        
    2.  Updates metadata fields for the specified area via an API.
        
    
*   **complete** - Marks the download as complete and updates metadata fields via an API. It also uses a new filename if one is available

[NextContent Check Modes Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/content-check-mode-args)

# Model Sorting & Processing Options | OF-Scraper

circle-info

**When a model is set to renew, the "expired" option refers to the renewal date**

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-sorting-args#sorting-criteria)

Sorting Criteria


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-sorting-args#st-sort-argument)

\-st, --sort \[argument\]

*   **Controls:** The order of the model list and processing order.
    
*   **Possible choices:**
    
    *   `name`: Sorts by model name (default).
        
    *   `subscribed`: Sorts by whether the model is currently subscribed
        
    *   `expired`: Sorts by the renewal date
        
    *   `current-price`: Sorts by the current price of the model.
        
    *   `promo-price`: Sorts by the promotional price of the model (if available).
        
    *   `regular-price`: Sorts by the regular price of the model (if available).
        
    *   `renew-price`: Sorts by the renewal price of the model (if applicable).
        
    *   `last-seen`: Sorts by the last time the model was seen
        
    
*   **Example:** With `-st expired`, models with expiring subscriptions will be processed first.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-sorting-args#ds-desc)

\-ds, --desc

*   **Arranges:** The model list in descending order.
    
*   **Default:** `False` (ascending order)
    
*   **Use case:** You might use this option to prioritize models at the bottom of the list (e.g., with `-st last-seen -ds`).
    

[PreviousUser Selection Optionschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/user-selection-options)
[NextContent Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Sorting Criteria](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-sorting-args#sorting-criteria)
    
*   [\-st, --sort \[argument\]](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-sorting-args#st-sort-argument)
    
*   [\-ds, --desc](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-sorting-args#ds-desc)

# Automation Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/general-scraper-args#background-execution)

Background Execution


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/general-scraper-args#d-daemon-argument)

\-d, --daemon \[argument\]

*   **Runs:** The program in the background as a daemon process.
    
*   **Argument:** (required) Specify the desired interval between program runs (e.g., `-d 60` for hourly runs).
    

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/general-scraper-args#automated-actions)

Automated Actions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/general-scraper-args#a-action-argument)

\-a, --action \[argument\]

*   **Selects:** The automated action to perform on posts.
    
*   **Possible choices:**
    
    *   `like`: Like each post encountered during processing.
        
    *   `unlike`: Unlike each post encountered during processing.
        
    *   `download`: Download media associated with each post encountered during processing.
        
    

**Combined actions:** You can combine the `-a` option multiple times to specify multiple actions. For example, `-a like -a download` or `a like,download` would like and download media for each post.

#### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/general-scraper-args#action-descriptions)

**Action Descriptions:**

circle-info

**Like and unlike are limited by rate limiting**

*   **Like:** Attempts to like each post processed by the program.
    
*   **Unlike:** Attempts to unlike each post processed by the program
    
*   **Download:** Downloads associated media (e.g., images, videos) from each post processed by the program
    

[PreviousContent Optionschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args)
[NextAdvanced Search & Processing Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/advanced-search-and-processing-options)

*   [Automated Actions](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/general-scraper-args#automated-actions)

# Program Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/global-args#general-options)

General Options


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/global-args#v-version)

\-v, --version

*   **Displays:** The program's version number and then exits.
    
*   **Example output:** `2.4.5+main.8f998cd` (This might vary depending on the actual version).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/global-args#cg-config-argument)

\-cg, --config \[argument\]

*   **Controls:** The location of the configuration folder or file.
    
*   **Default behavior:** The program uses the default configuration location
    
*   **Example:** With `-cg /custom/config/path`, the program will look for configuration files in the `/custom/config/path` directory
    

[Advanced Argschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/advanced-args)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/global-args#r-profile-argument-optional)

\-r, --profile \[argument\] (optional)

*   **Specifies:** The name of the profile directory, which stores authentication information
    

This is store in the config location

*   **Default behavior:** The program uses the default profile 'main'
    
*   **Example:** With `-r test`, the program will use a profile named test
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/global-args#env-file-path)

\--env-file \[path\]

*   **Specifies:** The path to an external `.env` file from which to load environment variables.
    
*   **Effect:** Variables defined in this file are loaded into the program's environment. Values from this file will **override** system environment variables that might be set. These values are then utilized by various configuration settings that are designed to read from environment variables.
    
*   **Default behavior:** If this option is not provided, the program automatically searches for a `.env` file in the current working directory and its parent directories.
    
*   **Example:** With `--env-file /home/user/my_app/prod.env`, the program will load environment variables from the specified `prod.env` file.
    

[Advanced Customizationchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/advanced-customization)

[NextLogging Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/logging)

Last updated 9 months ago

# Shared Scrape and Metadata Check Mode Options | OF-Scraper

Metadata mode and the main scraper serve distinct purposes, they share a foundation of common command-line arguments that govern their behavior The key difference lies in their goals: the main scraper focuses on downloading content, while Metadata mode leverages the API to gather and update information about user profiles and content within the program's internal tables

[PreviousScript Optionschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/script-options)
[NextUser List Filter Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args)

# Content Check Modes Options | OF-Scraper

circle-info

**Cached information is generally stored for around 3 days to improve efficiency**

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/content-check-mode-args#syntax)

Syntax


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    ofscraper [subcommand_name] [subcommand_options]

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/content-check-mode-args#example)

example

Copy

    ofscraper post_check --url test

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/content-check-mode-args#general-options)

General Options


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[General Program Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups)

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/content-check-mode-args#subcommand-options)

Subcommand Options


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each content check subcommand (`post_check`, `msg_check`, `paid_check`, `story_check`) accepts common arguments for specifying content sources and controlling update behavior.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/content-check-mode-args#specifying-content-source)

Specifying Content Source

*   **\-u, --url \[argument\]:** (all subcommands)
    
    *   Scans content from one or more URLs provided as arguments (separate URLs with spaces).
        
    
*   **\-f, --file \[argument\]:** (all subcommands)
    
    *   Scans content from a file containing entries (URLs or usernames) separated by lines.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/content-check-mode-args#forcing-update)

Forcing Update

*   **\-fo, --force \[argument\]:** (all subcommands)
    
    *   **Default:** `False` (uses cached data if available).
        
    *   Sets `True` to force the API to retrieve the latest information, bypassing the cache.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/content-check-mode-args#text)

Text

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/content-check-mode-args#tn-text-argument)

**\-tn, --text** \[argument\]

*   Specify to download text with any media tied to that text
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/content-check-mode-args#tp-text-only-argument)

**\-tp, --text-only** \[argument\]

*   Specify to download only text, skipping any media
    

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/content-check-mode-args#subcommand-descriptions)

Subcommand Descriptions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Here's a summary of each content check subcommand:**

*   **post\_check:** Analyzes data associated with posts from specified URLs or a file. It generates a table displaying relevant information about the posts.
    
*   **msg\_check:** Analyzes data associated with messages from specified URLs or a file. It generates a table displaying relevant information about the messages.
    
*   **paid\_check:** Analyzes data associated with purchased content from specified usernames or a file. It generates a table displaying relevant information about the purchased content.
    
*   **story\_check:** Analyzes data associated with stories and highlights from specified usernames or a file. It generates a table displaying relevant information about the stories/highlights.
    

[PreviousMetadata Check Mode Optionschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/metadata-check-mode-options)
[NextManual Mode Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/manual-mode-args)

Last updated 1 year ago

# User Selection Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/user-selection-options#specifying-usernames)

Specifying Usernames


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/user-selection-options#u-username-argument)

\-u, --username \[argument\]

*   **Selects:** Specific usernames to process, separated by commas (e.g., `name1,name2`).
    
*   **Case-sensitive:** Usernames are matched based on exact case.
    
*   **ALL (case-sensitive):** Use `ALL` to include all available usernames in the program's data.
    

**Example:** With `-u user1,user2`, only users "user1" and "user2" will be processed.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/user-selection-options#eu-excluded-username-argument)

\-eu, --excluded-username \[argument\]

*   **Excludes:** Specific usernames from processing, separated by commas (e.g., `name1,name2`).
    
*   **Precedence:** Excluded usernames take priority over usernames specified with `-u`.
    

**Example:** With `-u user1,user2` and `-eu user2`, only "user1" will be processed (excluding "user2").

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/user-selection-options#using-user-lists)

Using User Lists


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/user-selection-options#ul-user-list-argument-optional)

\-ul, --user-list \[argument\] (optional)

*   **Filters:** Users based on entries in a user list.
    
*   **Default list:** "ofscraper.main" (if no argument provided).
    
*   **Built-in lists:** The program also has built-in lists "ofscraper.active" and "ofscraper.disabled" corresponding to active and expired account respectively
    
*   **Argument behavior:**
    
    *   If no argument is provided, the default list ("scrape") will be used.
        
    *   If an argument is provided (e.g., "myuserList"), only the specified list will be processed.
        
    

**Example:** With `-ul myUserList`, only users in the "myUserList" list will be processed.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/user-selection-options#bl-black-list-argument-optional)

\-bl, --black-list \[argument\] (optional)

*   **Excludes:** Users based on entries in a user list.
    
*   **Blacklist behavior:** Similar to user lists, but excludes all users from the specified list
    
*   **Default list:** None
    
*   **Argument behavior:**
    
    *   If an argument is provided (e.g., "inactiveUsers"), only users from the specified blacklist will be excluded.
        
    

**Example:** With `-bl inactiveUsers`, users in the "inactiveUsers" blacklist will be excluded from processing

[PreviousAdvanced User Filterschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters)
[NextModel Sorting & Processing Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-sorting-args)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Specifying Usernames](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/user-selection-options#specifying-usernames)
    
*   [\-u, --username \[argument\]](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/user-selection-options#u-username-argument)
    
*   [\-eu, --excluded-username \[argument\]](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/user-selection-options#eu-excluded-username-argument)

*   [\-bl, --black-list \[argument\] (optional)](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/user-selection-options#bl-black-list-argument-optional)

# Advanced Search & Processing Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/advanced-search-and-processing-options#username-search-behavior)

Username Search Behavior


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These options control how usernames are searched for during program actions.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/advanced-search-and-processing-options#uf-users-first)

\-uf, --users-first

*   **Prioritizes:** Downloading posts by scraping all users at once instead of one at a time.
    
*   **Effect:** This allows for gathering all required data before downloading or processing metadata
    
*   **Default:** `False` (users are processed one by one)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/advanced-search-and-processing-options#fi-force-individual)

\-fi, --force-individual

*   **Enforces:** Searching each username provided with the `--username` argument as a separate request.
    
*   **Default:** This behavior depends on the number of --usernames and the number of subscriptions on account
    
*   **Use case:** This may be faster then retriving usernames in bulk
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/advanced-search-and-processing-options#fl-force-list)

\-fl, --force-list

*   **Processes:** The entire user list based on the currently enabled configuration settings for `userlist` or the `--user-list` argument.
    
*   **Effect:** Separates usernames within the list
    
*   **Default:** This behavior depends on the number of --usernames and the number of subscriptions on account
    
*   **Use case:** This is useful if your retriving a large number of users
    

**Note:** Using `-fi` might lead to a large number of individual requests, potentially overloading the target server or encountering rate limits.

[PreviousAutomation Optionschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/general-scraper-args)
[NextMain Scraper Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/main-scraper-options)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Username Search Behavior](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/advanced-search-and-processing-options#username-search-behavior)
    
*   [\-uf, --users-first](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/advanced-search-and-processing-options#uf-users-first)
    
*   [\-fi, --force-individual](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/advanced-search-and-processing-options#fi-force-individual)

# Logging Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/logging#log-levels)

Log Levels


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/logging#l-log-argument)

\-l, --log \[argument\]

*   **Possible choices:**
    
    *   `OFF`: Disables log output to the log file.
        
    *   `STATS`: Logs only high-level statistics and errors.
        
    *   `LOW`: Logs basic program flow and non-critical errors.
        
    *   `NORMAL` (default): Logs most program activity and errors.
        
    *   `DEBUG`: Logs all program activity and detailed debugging information.
        
    
*   **Sets:** The verbosity level for the program's log file.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/logging#dc-discord-argument)

\-dc, --discord \[argument\]

*   **Possible choices:**
    
    *   `OFF`: Disables log output to Discord.
        
    *   `STATS`: Logs only high-level statistics and errors to Discord.
        
    *   `LOW`: Logs basic program flow and non-critical errors to Discord.
        
    *   `NORMAL`: Logs most program activity and errors to Discord.
        
    *   `DEBUG`: Logs all program activity and detailed debugging information to Discord.
        
    
*   **Sets:** The verbosity level for logs sent to the Discord channel (if configured).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/logging#p-output-argument)

\-p, --output \[argument\]

*   **Possible choices:**
    
    *   `PROMPT`: Logs only critical information displayed on the program prompt.
        
    *   `STATS`: Logs only high-level statistics and errors to the console.
        
    *   `LOW`: Logs basic program flow and non-critical errors to the console.
        
    *   `NORMAL` (default): Logs most program activity and errors to the console.
        
    *   `DEBUG`: Logs all program activity and detailed debugging information to the console.
        
    
*   **Sets:** The verbosity level for log messages displayed in the console window.
    

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/logging#other-options)

Other Options


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/logging#nl-no-live)

**\-nl,--no-live**

*   **Controls**: Live displays via rich, these are used for Panels, Spinners, and progress bars
    
*   **Defaults**: False

# Media Filters Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options#media-type-filter)

Media Type Filter


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options#mt-mediatype-argument)

\-mt, --mediatype \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** media by type
    
*   **Possible Choices:**
    
    *   Audio
        
    *   Videos
        
    *   Images
        
    *   Text (Downloads Post Text)
        
    
*   **Defaults:** Audio, Video , Images
    
*   **Example:** -mt Images, only images will be downloaded
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options#file-size-filters)

File Size Filters


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options#sx-size-max-argument)

\-sx, --size-max \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Files exceeding the specified size.
    
*   **Accepts:** Human-readable size values like "10MB", "500GB", etc.
    
*   **Default:** `None` (no maximum size filter)
    
*   **Example:** With `-sx 1GB`, only files 1 gigabyte or smaller will be downloaded.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options#sm-size-min-argument)

\-sm, --size-min \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Files smaller than the specified size.
    
*   **Accepts:** Human-readable size values like "10MB", "500GB", etc.
    
*   **Default:** `None` (no minimum size filter)
    
*   **Example:** With `-sm 50MB`, only files 50 megabytes or larger will be downloaded.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options#media-length-filters-video-only)

Media Length Filters (Video Only)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These filters only apply to video files.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options#lx-length-max-argument)

\-lx, --length-max \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Videos longer than the specified duration.
    
*   **Accepts:** Values that will be interpreted as seconds
    
*   **Default:** `None` (no maximum length filter)
    
*   **Example:** With `-lx 30`, only videos shorter or equal to 30 seconds will be downloaded.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options#lm-length-min-argument)

\-lm, --length-min \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Videos shorter than the specified duration.
    
*   **Accepts:** Values that will be intepreted as seconds
    
*   **Default:** `None` (no minimum length filter)
    
*   **Example:** With `-lm 5`, only videos 5 seconds or longer will be downloaded.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options#media-quality-filter)

Media Quality Filter


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options#q-quality-argument)

\-q, --quality \[argument\]

*   **Sets:** The minimum acceptable video quality
    
*   **Possible choices:**
    
    *   `source`: Attempts to download the highest available quality (may not always be achievable).
        
    *   `240`: Filters for videos with a resolution of at least 240p.
        
    *   `720`: Filters for videos with a resolution of at least 720p.
        
    
*   **Default:** `source` (attempts to download highest quality)
    
*   **Note:** The program might download a higher quality version if the specified quality is unavailable
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options#media-id-filter)

Media ID Filter


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/media-filters-options#md-media-id-argument)

\-md,--media-id \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** filters based on mediaid
    
*   **Default:** None
    
*   **Note:** This will have no effect on search speed, as filtering must be done after all posts are found

# Script Options | OF-Scraper

[Script Optionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/script-options)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/script-options#ds-after-action-script-argument)

\-ds, --after-action-script \[argument\]

**Executes:** A user-defined script after an action is completed on a model

**Runs:**

*   rafter each model is downloaded in the main scraper
    
*   after each model's metadata is processed in metadata mode
    
*   after each model is processed in manual mode
    
*   for each unique model, after the current cart is downloaded in check mode
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/script-options#ps-post-script-argument)

\-ps, --post-script \[argument\]

**Executes:** A user-defined script once the script finishes an action

**Runs:**

*   once all models are downloaded or liked in scrape mode
    
*   once all the post from manual mode are completed
    
*   After the current cart downloads are processed in check mode, and after the download-script is processed for each user
    
*   after all metadata for all users is processed in metadata mode
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/script-options#ns-naming-script-argument)

\-ns, --naming-script \[argument\]

**Executes:** A script that dynamically generates the final filename

**Runs:**

*   when the temporary .part filename is generated for a download
    
*   when the final filename is being generated for a download
    
*   when the final filename is being generated for a text download
    
*   after all metadata for all users is processed in metadata mode
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/script-options#sdl-skip-download-script-argument)

\-sdl, --skip-download-script \[argument\]

**Executes:** A script that determines whether to skip or continue a download

**Runs:**

*   Just before a download starts
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/script-options#adl-after-download-script-argument)

\-adl, --after-download-script \[argument\]

**Executes:** A script that runs after a download has completed

**Runs:**

*   Just before a download starts

*   [\-ps, --post-script \[argument\]](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/script-options#ps-post-script-argument)

# Advanced Program Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/advanced-args#caching-and-api-calls)

Caching and API Calls


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/advanced-args#nc-no-cache)

\-nc, --no-cache

*   **Disables:** Reading from and writing to the program's cache.
    
*   **Effect:** Disables all uses of cache including For example cache is used to store keys and file sizes Also forces the program to make fresh sequential API calls for data, even if it's available in the cache. This can be useful for ensuring you have the latest information but can be slower than using the cache
    
*   **Default:** `False` (cache is enabled)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/advanced-args#nca-no-api-cache)

\-nca, --no-api-cache

*   **Effect:** Forces the program to make sequential API calls for data, even if it's cached within the current program session. This is different from `--no-cache` which is for all uses of the cache library beyond just OF API request
    
*   **Default:** `False` (API cache is enabled for the current session)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/advanced-args#configuration-overrides)

Configuration Overrides


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/advanced-args#k-key-mode-argument)

\-k, --key-mode \[argument\]

*   **Overrides:** The key mode setting specified in the configuration file.
    
*   **Possible values:**
    
    *   cdrm
        
    *   manual
        
    
*   **Requires Argument:** You must specify the desired key mode after the option (e.g., `-k manual`).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/advanced-args#dr-dynamic-rules-argument)

\-dr, --dynamic-rules \[argument\]

*   **Overrides:** The `dynamic-rules` setting in the configuration file.
    
*   **Used for:** Signing API requests.
    
*   **Default:** `false` (dynamic rules are disabled)
    
*   **Possible values:**
    
    *   sneaky
        
    *   digital
        
    *   deviint
        
    
*   **Requires Argument:** You must specify a value for dynamic rules (e.g., `-dr sneaky`)
    
*   **Note:** Possible values may change based on removal of sources, frequency of updates of sources
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/advanced-args#additional-options)

Additional Options


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/advanced-args#up-update-profile)

\-up, --update-profile

*   **Retrieves:** Up-to-date profile information directly from the API, bypassing the cache.
    
*   **Cache Update:** Profile information is typically cached for about a day. Use this option if you need the absolute latest data.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/advanced-args#al-auth-fail)

\-al, --auth-fail

*   quit on authentication failure rather then prompting
    
*   **Default:** False

# Advanced User Filters | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#advanced-pricing-filters)

Advanced Pricing Filters


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These filters allow you to target accounts based on specific price ranges for different pricing models (promotional, regular, current, and renewal

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#ppm-promo-price-max-argument)

\-ppm, --promo-price-max \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts where the lowest available promotional price matches or falls below the specified value
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#ppn-promo-price-min-argument)

\-ppn, --promo-price-min \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts where the lowest available promotional price matches or falls above the specified value
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#gpm-regular-price-max-argument)

\-gpm, --regular-price-max \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts where the regular price (if available) matches or falls below the specified value
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#gpn-regular-price-min-argument)

\-gpn, --regular-price-min \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts where the regular price (if available) matches or falls above the specified value
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#cpm-current-price-max-argument)

\-cpm, --current-price-max \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts where the current price matches or falls below the specified value
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#cpn-current-price-min-argument)

\-cpn, --current-price-min \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts where the current price matches or falls above the specified value
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#rpm-renewal-price-max-argument)

\-rpm, --renewal-price-max \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts where the renewal price (if applicable) matches or falls below the specified value
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#rpn-renewal-price-min-argument)

\-rpn, --renewal-price-min \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts where the renewal price (if applicable) matches or falls above the specified value
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#advanced-account-attributes)

Advanced Account Attributes


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These filters allow you to target accounts based on specific dates related to their activity or subscription status

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fof-scraper.gitbook.io%2Fof-scraper%2F%7Egitbook%2Ficon%3Fsize%3Dsmall%26theme%3Dlight&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff8d559f&sv=2)Downloading Content | OF-Scraperof-scraper.gitbook.iochevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/selecting-posts#valid-inputs)

Valid Date Inputs

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#lsa-last-seen-after-argument)

\-lsa, --last-seen-after \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts where the "last seen" date/time is at or after the provided date
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#lsb-last-seen-before-argument)

\-lsb, --last-seen-before \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts where the "last seen" date/time is at or before the provided date
    

**Note:** The "last seen" date/time might not be available for all accounts

circle-info

**When a model is set to renew, the expired date refers to the renewal date**

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#ea-expire-after-argument)

\-ea, --expire-after \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts with an expiration or renewal date at or after the provided date
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#eb-expire-before-argument)

\-eb, --expire-before \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts with an expiration or renewal date at or before the provided date
    

circle-info

**The subscription date might not always be the most accurate indicator for expired accounts. Consider using the** `**-ea**` **or** `**-eb**` **filters instead.**

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#sa-subscribed-after-argument)

\-sa, --subscribed-after \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts with a subscription date at or after the provided date
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args/advanced-user-filters#sb-subscribed-before-argument)

\-sb, --subscribed-before \[argument\]

*   **Filters:** Accounts with a subscription date at or before the provided date

# Download Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/download-options#download-configuration-overrides)

Download Configuration Overrides


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**For threads and sems**

[Values to Pickchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options/performance-options/values-to-pick)

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/download-options#db-download-bars)

\-db, --download-bars

*   **Overrides:** The `downloadbars` setting in the configuration file
    
*   **Default:** `None`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/download-options#sd-download-sems-argument)

\-sd, --download-sems \[argument\]

*   **Overrides:** The `download_sems` setting in the configuration file. This setting controls the number of concurrent download processes.
    
*   **Default:** `None` (uses default value from configuration file)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/download-options#dt-download-threads-argument)

\-dt, --download-threads \[argument\]

*   **Overrides:** The `threads_count` setting in the configuration file. This setting controls the number of threads used within each download process.
    
*   **Special case:** Setting the value to zero forces the program to use the main thread for downloading. The main thread is also used if there aren't enough active downloads to fill the configured number of download threads.
    
*   **Default:** `None` (uses default value from configuration file)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/download-options#dl-download-limit-argument)

\-dl, --download-limit\[argument\]

*   **Overrides:** The `download_limit` setting in the configuration file.
    
*   **Limits:** the maximum download speed per thread to the specified number of bytes per second
    
*   **Accepts:** Human-readable size values like "10MB"
    
*   **Default:** No default limit (unlimited download speed).
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/download-options#download-cleanup)

Download Cleanup


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/common-option-groups/download-options#ar-no-auto-resume)

\-ar, --no-auto-resume


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Disables:** Automatic cleanup of partially downloaded files (".part" files) upon program exit. This includes forced exits (e.g., Ctrl+C).
    
*   **Default:** `false` (automatic cleanup is enabled)
    

* * *
