# User List Filter Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#pricing-filters)

Pricing Filters


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

**Refer to the dedicated documentation for detailed information on price filtering and sorting**

[Price Filtering/Sortchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/model-selection-sorting/price-filtering-sort)

These options allow you to filter accounts based on their current price, renewal price, promotional price (if available), and regular price (if available).

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#cp-current-price-argument)

\-cp, --current-price \[argument\]

*   **Possible choices:**
    
    *   `paid`: Filters for accounts with a paid current price.
        
    *   `free`: Filters for accounts with a free current price.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#rp-renewal-price-argument)

\-rp, --renewal-price \[argument\]

*   **Possible choices:**
    
    *   `paid`: Filters for accounts with a paid renewal price.
        
    *   `free`: Filters for accounts with a free renewal price.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#pp-promo-price-argument)

\-pp, --promo-price \[argument\]

*   **Possible choices:**
    
    *   `paid`: Filters for accounts with a claimable promotional price.
        
    *   `free`: Filters for accounts without a claimable promotional price.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#gp-regular-price-argument)

\-gp, --regular-price \[argument\]

*   **Possible choices:**
    
    *   `paid`: Filters for accounts with a regular price (if applicable).
        
    *   `free`: Filters for accounts without a regular price (if applicable).
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#account-flags)

Account Flags


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These options filter accounts based on specific flags or properties.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#lo-last-seen-only)

\-lo, --last-seen-only

*   **Filters:** Accounts where the "last seen" date/time is visible.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#ls-last-seen-skip)

\-ls, --last-seen-skip

*   **Filters:** Accounts where the "last seen" date/time is hidden.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#po-promo-only)

\-po, --promo-only

*   **Filters:** Accounts with any claimable promotional price.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#ps-promo-skip)

\-ps, --promo-skip

*   **Filters:** Accounts without any claimable promotional price.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#ao-all-promo-only)

\-ao, --all-promo-only

*   **Filters:** Accounts with any claimable promotional price, regardless of current or renewal status.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#as-all-promo-skip)

\-as, --all-promo-skip

*   **Filters:** Accounts without any claimable promotional price, regardless of current or renewal status.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#subscription-type)

Subscription Type


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These options filter accounts based on their subscription status.

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#fo-free-trial-only)

\-fo, --free-trial-only

*   **Filters:** Accounts currently in a free trial (normally paid accounts).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#fs-free-trial-skip)

\-fs, --free-trial-skip

*   **Filters:** Accounts that are not currently in a free trial (normally paid accounts).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#ts-active-subscriptions)

\-ts, --active-subscriptions

*   **Filters:** Accounts with active, non-expired subscriptions.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#es-expired-subscription)

\-es, --expired-subscription

*   **Filters:** Accounts with expired subscriptions.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#ro-renew-on)

\-ro, --renew-on

*   **Filters:** Accounts with the "renew" flag enabled.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-filter-args#rf-renew-off)

\-rf, --renew-off

*   **Filters:** Accounts with the "renew" flag disabled.

# Setting metadata path | OF-Scraper

In the config.json file, you can modify the default metadata location or adjust where the script searches for database files

Using your existing metadata files from DIGITALCRIMINALS' script enables immediate utilization of the dupe checker, with any new files added subsequently being appended to the existing ones

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/setting-metadata-path#config-file-location)

Config File Location


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Config Locationchevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/config-location)

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/setting-metadata-path#changing-metadata-location)

Changing metadata location


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Adjust the metadata section in the config.json file by inserting the appropriate locations or paths using the provided placeholders

Copy

    {sitename} = Onlyfans
    
    {first_letter} = first letter of model's username
    
    {model_username} = The model's username.
    
    {model_id}= Unique identification number for model
    {config_path}= The directory containing the config.json file
    {profile} =The currently active profile
    {save_location} = This option retrieves the parsed path specified in the 'save_location' 
    option
    {my_username}=The authorized account's username
    {my_id} = The identification number assigned to the authorized account
    
    {current_price}= Free if current price is 0 dollars else paid
    {regular_price}=Free if regular price is 0 dollars else paid
    {promo_price}= Free if promo price is 0 dollars else paid
    {renewal_price}= Free if renewal price is 0 dollars else paid

[PreviousExample Configschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/example-configs)
[NextOptionschevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/options)

Last updated 9 months ago

*   [Config File Location](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/setting-metadata-path#config-file-location)
    
*   [Changing metadata location](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/getting-started/config-options/setting-metadata-path#changing-metadata-location)

# Content Options | OF-Scraper

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#targeting-content)

Targeting Content


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#o-posts-argument)

**\-o, --posts** \[argument\]

*   Specify the type of content to target for actions (like, unlike, download).
    
*   **Possible choices:** `highlights`, `all`, `archived`, `messages`, `timeline`, `pinned`, `stories`, `purchased`, `profile`, `labels`.
    
*   **Defaults:** to `None`.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#t-text-argument)

**\-t, --text** \[argument\]

*   Specify the type of content to target for text download
    
*   **Note:** This only has an effect on action download
    
*   **Possible choices:** `highlights`, `all`, `archived`, `messages`, `timeline`, `pinned`, `stories`, `purchased`, `profile`, `labels`.
    
*   **Defaults:** to `None`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#la-like-area-argument)

**\-la, --like-area** \[argument\]

*   Define the area for like/unlike actions (overrides `--posts`).
    
*   **Possible choices:** `all`, `archived`, `timeline`, `pinned`, `stories`, `labels`.
    
*   **Defaults**: to `None`.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#da-download-area-argument)

**\-da, --download-area** \[argument\]

*   Specify the area for download actions (overrides `--posts`).
    
*   **Possible choices:** `highlights`, `all`, `archived`, `messages`, `timeline`, `pinned`, `stories`, `purchased`, `profile`, `labels`.
    
*   **Defaults** to `None`.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#filtering-content)

Filtering Content


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#sk-skip-timed)

**\-sk, --skip-timed**

*   Skips temporary posts (commonly used for promotions).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#ms-mass-skip)

**\-ms, --mass-skip**

*   Filters downloads to include only those labeled as mass messages.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#mm-mass-msg)

**\-mm, --mass-msg**

*   Excludes downloads marked as mass messages.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#ok-only-timed)

**\-ok, --only-timed**

*   Downloads only temporary posts (mostly used for promotions).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#ft-filter-argument)

**\-ft, --filter** \[argument\]

*   Filter posts using a provided regular expression pattern.
    
*   Case-sensitive if uppercase characters are included.
    
*   Posts matching the pattern are included.
    
*   **Defaults:** to `".*"` (matches all posts).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#nf-neg-filter-argument)

**\-nf, --neg-filter** \[argument\]

*   Filter posts to exclude based on a regular expression pattern.
    
*   Case-sensitive if uppercase characters are included.
    
*   Posts matching the pattern are excluded.
    
*   **Defaults:** to `None` (no exclusion)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#to-protected-only)

**\-to, --protected-only**

*   Restricts downloads to content requiring decryption.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#no-normal-only)

**\-no, --normal-only**

*   Restricts downloads to content that does not require decryption.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#lb-label)

**\-lb, --label**

*   Scrape content with specific labels.
    
*   **Defaults:** to `None` (no specific label).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#pd-post-id-argument)

**\-pd, --post-id \[argument\]**

*   Filters content based on post ID
    
*   **Arguments:** One or more comma-separated (",") post IDs. You can also provide URLs containing a valid post ID
    
*   **Defaults:** None
    
*   **Note:** In certain situation this will allow direct search of content, namely for timeline and message related posts and if the number is less then 10
    
*   **Note:** you can also use manual if you want to process post for multiple users
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#tls-timeline-strict)

\-tls, --timeline-strict

*   Filters timeline to only include non-pinned and non-archived posts
    
*   **Default: False**
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#a-d-filter)

AD Filter


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#ba-block-a-ds)

**\-ba, --block-ads**

*   Filter posts with regex to block posts with common words for advertisements
    
*   **Regex :**
    

**Note:** This is passed as a raw string when being used by python

*   **Defaults:** None
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#nf-neg-filter-argument-1)

**\-nf, --neg-filter** \[argument\]

*   Filter posts to exclude based on a regular expression pattern.
    
*   Case-sensitive if uppercase characters are included.
    
*   Posts matching the pattern are excluded.
    
*   **Defaults:** to `None` (no exclusion)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#date-range)

Date Range

[![Logo](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fof-scraper.gitbook.io%2Fof-scraper%2F%7Egitbook%2Ficon%3Fsize%3Dsmall%26theme%3Dlight&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff8d559f&sv=2)Downloading Content | OF-Scraperof-scraper.gitbook.iochevron-right](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/using-the-scraper/batch-scraping-and-bot-actions/selecting-posts#valid-inputs)

Valid Date Inputs

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#be-before-argument)

**\-be, --before** \[argument\]

*   Process posts on or before a specified date (format: Month/Day/Year).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#af-after-argument)

**\-af, --after** \[argument\]

*   Process posts on or after a specified date (format: Month/Day/Year).
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#other-options)

Other Options


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#e-force-all)

**\-e, --force-all**

*   Downloads all files regardless of database presence.
    
*   **Defaults:** to `False`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#fl-force-like)

**\-fl,--force-like**

*   Like posts regardless of status in cache
    
*   **Defaults:** to `False`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#eq-force-model-unique)

**\-eq, --force-model-unique**

*   Downloads files only if not present for the current model
    
*   **Defaults:** to `False`.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#sp-scrape-paid)

**\-sp, --scrape-paid**

*   Scrapes the entire paid page for content (can be time-consuming).
    
*   **Defaults:** to `False`.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#it-item-sort-argument)

**\-it, --item-sort** \[argument\]

*   Defines the order for processing media sort order before actions.
    
*   Uses default action sorting if `None`.
    
*   **Defaults are:**
    
    *   Date for likes/unlikes (always)
        
    *   Date for normal downloader
        
    *   Shuffled for batch downlooader
        
    
*   **Possible choices:**
    
    *   `random`: Randomize order
        
    *   `text-asc`: Sort by post text in ascending order
        
    *   `text-desc`: Sort by post text in descending order
        
    *   `date-asc`: Sort by media date in ascending order
        
    *   `date-desc`: Sort by media date in descending order
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/post-filter-args#xc-max-count-argument)

**\-xc ,--max-count** \[argument\]

*   Sets the maximum number of posts to like or download.
    
*   **Defaults:** to `None` (no limit).
    

[PreviousModel Sorting & Processing Optionschevron-left](https://of-scraper.gitbook.io/of-scraper/command-reference/shared-options/scrape-metadata-options/account-sorting-args)
